### 2.3 项目环境配置

创建logs scripts目录，

在xiaofu下创建libs,utils,settings python包，注意是Python包不是目录包含\_\_init__.py文件，settings目录下创建dev.py以及prod.py分别代表生产和开发环境

![](水印pics\创建各类目录.png)

修改dev.py

修改时间，文字，还有sys.path添加路径

```
import sys,os
# sys.path保存了python解释器的导包路径，默认从manage.py同级目录下寻找
sys.path.insert(0,os.path.join(BASE_DIR,'apps'))

LANGUAGE_CODE = 'zh-hans'

TIME_ZONE = 'Asia/Shanghai'
```



创建users app

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py startapp users

```



```
如果之前我们不添加sys.path.insert(0,os.path.join(BASE_DIR,'apps')) 则在devs.py下的
INSTALLED_APPS需要这么写
'xiaofu.apps.users'

加如sys.path后可以直接写users
```

在dev.py下 INSTALLED_APPS中添加

```
INSTALLED_APPS = [
    ...
    'rest_framework',
    'users'
]
```

修改dev.py 添加redis配置

保证redis数据库没有开启密码

```
# 设置Django缓存(如果不做设置，Django默认缓存是服务器的内存)
# 缓存中可以有多个存储空间
CACHES = {
    "default": {
        "BACKEND": "django_redis.cache.RedisCache",
        "LOCATION": "redis://192.168.70.101:6379/0",
        "OPTIONS": {
            "CLIENT_CLASS": "django_redis.client.DefaultClient",
        }
    },
    "session": {
        "BACKEND": "django_redis.cache.RedisCache",
        "LOCATION": "redis://192.168.70.101:6379/1",
        "OPTIONS": {
            "CLIENT_CLASS": "django_redis.client.DefaultClient",
        }
    }
}

# 指定将session存储到缓存中
SESSION_ENGINE = "django.contrib.sessions.backends.cache"
# 指定将session存储到缓存哪个空间中,这里主要给django admin提供的
SESSION_CACHE_ALIAS = "session"
```



##### 2.4.3 数据库异常处理

新建utils/exceptions.py

```python
from rest_framework.views import exception_handler as drf_exception_handler
from django.db import DatabaseError
from redis.exceptions import RedisError
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework import status

import logging

# 获取在配置文件中定义的logger，用来记录日志
logger = logging.getLogger('django')


def exception_handler(exc, context):
    """
    自定义异常处理
    :param exc: 异常
    :param context: 抛出异常的上下文
    :return: Response响应对象
    """
    # 调用drf框架原生的异常处理方法
    response = drf_exception_handler(exc, context)

    if response is None:
        view = context['view']
        # 判断redis或者mysql数据库异常
        if isinstance(exc, DatabaseError) or isinstance(exc, RedisError):
            # 数据库异常
            logger.error('[%s] %s' % (view, exc))
            response = Response({'message': '服务器内部错误'}, status=status.HTTP_507_INSUFFICIENT_STORAGE)

    return response

```

修改settings/dev.py添加异常处理

```
REST_FRAMEWORK = {
    # 指定DRF框架异常处理函数
    'EXCEPTION_HANDLER': 'xiaofu.utils.exceptions.exception_handler',
}
```



### 2.5 日志配置

修改dev.py添加日志

```
# Django项目日志存储设置
LOGGING = {
    'version': 1,
    'disable_existing_loggers': False,  # 是否禁用已经存在的日志器
    'formatters': {  # 日志信息显示的格式
        'verbose': { # 详细日志
            'format': '%(levelname)s %(asctime)s %(module)s %(lineno)d %(message)s'
        },
        'simple': { # 简单日志
            'format': '%(levelname)s %(module)s %(lineno)d %(message)s'
        },
    },
    'filters': {  # 对日志过滤
        'require_debug_true': {  # django在debug模式下才输出日志
            '()': 'django.utils.log.RequireDebugTrue',
        },
    },
    'handlers': {  # 日志处理方法
        'console': {  # 向终端输出日志
            'level': 'INFO',
            'filters': ['require_debug_true'],
            'class': 'logging.StreamHandler',
            'formatter': 'simple'
        },
        'file': {  # 向文件输出日志
            'level': 'INFO',
            'class': 'logging.handlers.RotatingFileHandler',
            'filename': os.path.join(os.path.dirname(BASE_DIR), "logs/xiaofu.log"),  # 日志文件的位置
            'maxBytes': 100 * 1024 * 1024,
            'backupCount': 10,
            'formatter': 'verbose'
        },
    },
    'loggers': {  # 日志器
        'django': {  # 定义了一个名为django的日志器
            'handlers': ['console', 'file'],  # 可以同时向终端与文件中输出日志
            'propagate': True,  # 是否继续传递日志信息
            'level': 'INFO',  # 日志器接收的最低日志级别
        },
    }
}
```

# 3 用户app

使用Django认证系统，继承AbstractUser并且添加手机好mobile字段

users/models.py

```
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
# Create your models here.

class User(AbstractUser):
    mobile = models.CharField(max_length=11,unique=True, verbose_name='手机号码')

    class Meta:
        db_table = 'tb_users'
        verbose_name = '用户表'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

```

在dev.py添加

```
# Django认证所使用到的模型类,user代表应用名字User代表模型类名字
# 本来应该是users.model.User现在直接简写为users.User
AUTH_USER_MODEL = 'users.User'
```

# 4 注册

### 4.1 短信验证码

**处理步骤**

1. 检查手机号是否合法
2. 60秒内是否有发送记录
3. 生成6位短信验证码
4. 保存短信验证码与发送记录
5. 发送短信

**接口设计**

GET  /sms/{mobile}

| 参数   | 类型 | 说明   |
| ------ | ---- | ------ |
| mobile | str  | 手机号 |

返回数据 json

| 返回值 | 类型 | 说明                   |
| ------ | ---- | ---------------------- |
| res    | str  | OK, 短信验证码发送成功 |

##### 4.1.1 配置信息

新建app verifications

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py startapp verifications
```



在dev.py redis配置地方添加如下短信验证码信息

需要

```
# 短信验证码
    "verify_codes": {
        "BACKEND": "django_redis.cache.RedisCache",
        "LOCATION": "redis://192.168.70.101:6379/2",
        "OPTIONS": {
            "CLIENT_CLASS": "django_redis.client.DefaultClient",
        }
    }
```



新建verifications/serializers.py(**不需要此步了，这里就了解下mobile参数可以从context里面获取**)

添加短信验证逻辑

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from django_redis import get_redis_connection

class checkSmsCodeSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    '''
    校验短信验证码
    '''
    # redis中维护60秒的发送短信有效期的标志sms_flag_{mobile}
    # 通过get_serializer返回一个序列化器对象，restframework会象对象里面的context属性补充三个数据
    # request, format(前端请求的数据格式),view(当前类视图对象本身), 这三个对象可以在定义序列化器时候使用
    # 我们的路径参数mobile放在view视图对象下面
    def validate(self, attrs):
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('verify_codes')

        mobile = self.context['view'].kwargs['mobile']
        sms_flag = redis_conn.get('sms_flag_%s' %mobile)
        if sms_flag:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('发送短信过于频繁')


```



##### 4.1.2 容联云发送短信

<https://www.yuntongxun.com/member/main> 容联云官网

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 ~]$ pip install  -i https://pypi.tuna.tsinghua.edu.cn/simple ronglian_sms_sdk
```

新建libs/sms_code.py

```
from ronglian_sms_sdk import SmsSDK

# accId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b5bb1001'
# accToken = '153...5e7c6'
# appId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b6b01007'


class Sms():
    def __init__(self, accId, accToken, appId):
        self.accId = accId
        self.accToken = accToken
        self.appId = appId

    def send_message(self,tid,mobile,datas):
        sdk = SmsSDK(self.accId, self.accToken, self.appId)
        # tid = '1'
        # mobile = '13666668888'
        # datas = ('123453', '2')
        # datas[0]为短信验证码，datas[1]是多少时间内需要正确输入

        resp = sdk.sendMessage(tid, mobile, datas)

        return resp



if __name__ == "__main__":
    sms_obj = Sms('8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b5bb1001', '153d19a21d8b4b7fb9ec22121435e7c6',
                       '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b6b01007')
    sms_obj.send_message('1','13818377606',('123453', '222'))
```



##### 4.1.3 后端实现短信发送功能

新建libs/sms_constants.py

```
accId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b5bb1001'
accToken = '153...5e7c6'
appId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b6b01007'
```





新建verifications/constants.py

```
# 短信验证码有效期
SMS_CODE_EXPIRE = 300

# 短信发送间隔
SMS_CODE_INTERVAL = 60

# 短信模板ID
SMS_TEMPLATE_ID = 1
```





修改verifications/views.py

```
from django.shortcuts import render
from django_redis import get_redis_connection
from rest_framework.generics import GenericAPIView
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework import status

import random,json
# 获取logger
import logging
logger = logging.getLogger('django')

from . import constants
from xiaofu.libs.sms_code import Sms
from xiaofu.libs.sms_constants import accId,appId,accToken

# Create your views here.
# GET /sms_codes/(?P<mobile>1[3-9]\d{9})/
class SmsCodeView(GenericAPIView):
    def get(self, request, mobile):
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('verify_codes')

        # 检查短信是否发送过于频繁
        sms_flag = redis_conn.get('sms_flag_%s' % mobile)
        if sms_flag:
            return Response({'message': '发送短信过于频繁'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        # 6位数随机验证码
        sms_code = '%6d' % random.randint(100000,999999)

        # 设置短信有效期
        redis_conn.setex('sms_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, sms_code)
        # 设置短信发送间隔
        redis_conn.setex('sms_flag_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL,1)

        # 发送短信验证码
        sms_obj = Sms(accId, accToken, appId)
        sms_valid_time = int(constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE / 60)
        sms_resp = json.loads(sms_obj.send_message(constants.SMS_TEMPLATE_ID,mobile, [sms_code, sms_valid_time]))
        print("sms_resp",sms_resp,type(sms_resp))
        if sms_resp['statusCode'] != "000000":
            logger.error('手机号%s发送短信异常, 错误代码%s, 错误信息%s' % (mobile,sms_resp['statusCode'],sms_resp['statusMsg']))
            return Response({'message': '发送短信异常'}, status=status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE)

        return Response({'message':"发送短信验证码成功"})



```

修改最外层urls.py，添加verifications.urls路由

```
from django.contrib import admin
from django.urls import path,include, re_path

urlpatterns = [
    path('admin/', admin.site.urls),
    # verifications
    path('', include('verifications.urls'))
]
```



新建verifications/urls.py

```
from django.urls import path,include,re_path
from verifications import views

urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'sms/(?P<mobile>1[3-9]\d{9})/$', views.SmsCodeView.as_view()),
]
```



修改dev.py

```
ALLOWED_HOSTS = ['*']
```

##### 4.1.4 使用redisPipline一次执行多个命令

```
 # 注释掉如下代码
 # # 设置短信有效期
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, sms_code)
        # # 设置短信发送间隔
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_flag_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL,1)
```



```
# 修改为如下pipeline代码
# 建立管道
        pl = redis_conn.pipeline()
        # 批量执行命令
        pl.setex('sms_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, sms_code)
        pl.setex('sms_flag_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL,1)
        # 执行管道命令
        pl.execute()
```

    import RegFooter from '@/components/common/OperFooter.vue'

    import Info from '@/components/Account/Register/RegInfo'
    import Done from '@/components/Account/Register/Done'

        name: "Register",
        data() {
            return {
                active: 0,          // 当前的步骤

            };
        },
        components: {
            Sms,
            Info,
            Done,
            RegHeader,
            RegFooter
        },

            if (this.active==1){
                this.currentCom = 'Info'
            }
            if (this.active==2){
                this.currentCom = 'Done'
                this.active = 3
            }
        },
        
    }

                required: true,
                default: []

添加发送短信逻辑

```
<template>
    <div class="info-form">
        <el-form ref="formValidate" label-position="right" :model="formValidate" label-width="80px" :rules="ruleValidate">
            <el-form-item label="手机号" prop="phone">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.phone" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请输入手机号"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="验证码" prop="sms_code">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.sms_code" size="large"  placeholder="请输入验证码">
                    <el-button style="width:150px" :disabled="sms_disable" ref="sms_button" slot="append" @click="getSmsCode">{{sms_code_tip}}</el-button>
                </el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-button type="danger"  style="width: 100%"  @click="handleSubmit('formValidate')">下一步</el-button>
        </el-form>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    import axios from 'axios'
    export default {
        name: "Sms",
        data () {
            return {
                formValidate: {
                    phone: '',
                    sms_code: ''
                },
                ruleValidate: {
                    phone: [
                        { required: true, message: '手机号不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', pattern: /^1[3|4|5|7|8][0-9]{9}$/, message: '手机号格式出错', trigger: 'blur' }
                    ],
                    sms_code: [
                        { required: true, message: '请填写验证码', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', min: 6, max: 6, message: '验证码长度错误', trigger: 'blur' }
                    ]
                },
                sms_code_tip: "获取短信验证码",
                sms_disable: false

            };
        },
        methods: {
            getSmsCode () {
                this.$refs['formValidate'].validateField('phone', errMsg => {
                    if (!errMsg) {
                        let second = 10;
                        this.sms_code_tip = second + '秒';
                        let t = setInterval(() => {
                            if (second === 1) { // 倒计时即将结束
                                clearInterval(t); // 停止回调函数的执行
                                this.sms_disable = false
                                this.sms_code_tip = '获取短信验证码'; // 还原sms_code_tip的提示文字
                            } else { // 正在倒计时
                                second -= 1; // num = num - 1;
                                this.sms_code_tip = second + '秒';
                                this.sms_disable = true
                            }
                        }, 1000)
                        let mobile = this.formValidate.phone
                        axios.get('http://192.168.70.102:8000/sms/' + mobile).then(res => {
                            console.log(res)
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            console.log("错误信息",err)
                        })
                    } else {
                        return false;
                    }
                });



            },
            handleSubmit(name) {

            }
        },
    }
</script>

<style lang="stylus" scoped>
    .info-form
        width 80%

</style>
```

INSTALLED_APPS = [

]



MIDDLEWARE = [
	'corsheaders.middleware.CorsMiddleware',      # 中间件添加CorsMiddleware
    'django.middleware.security.SecurityMiddleware',
    'django.contrib.sessions.middleware.SessionMiddleware',
    'django.middleware.common.CommonMiddleware',
    'django.middleware.csrf.CsrfViewMiddleware',
    'django.contrib.auth.middleware.AuthenticationMiddleware',
    'django.contrib.messages.middleware.MessageMiddleware',
    'django.middleware.clickjacking.XFrameOptionsMiddleware',
]


# 添加如下信息

```

##### 4.1.9 封装短信发送组件

新建Account/common/Sms.vue

```
<template>
    <div class="info-form">
        <el-form :ref="formName" label-position="right" :model="formValidate" label-width="80px" :rules="ruleValidate">
            <el-form-item label="手机号" prop="phone">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.phone" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请输入手机号" :disabled="disabled_flag"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="验证码" prop="sms_code">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.sms_code" size="large"  placeholder="请输入验证码">
                    <el-button style="width:150px" :disabled="sms_disable" ref="sms_button" slot="append" @click="getSmsCode">{{sms_code_tip}}</el-button>
                </el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-button type="danger"  style="width: 100%"  @click="submit('formValidate')">下一步</el-button>
        </el-form>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    export default {
        name: "Sms",
        props: {
            disabled_flag: {
                type: Boolean,
                required: false,
                default: false
            },
            sms_disable: {
                type: Boolean,
                required: true,
                default: false
            },
            sms_code_tip: {
                type: String,
                required: true,
                default: "获取短信验证码"
            },
            ruleValidate: {
                type: Object,
                required: false,
                default: function () {
                    return {}
                }
            },
            formValidate: {
                type: Object,
                required: true,
                default: function () {
                    return {}
                }
            }
        },
        data () {
            return {
                formName: 'regForm'
            }
        },
        methods: {
            getSmsCode() {
                this.$emit('handleGetSmsCode',this.formName)
            },
            submit() {
                this.$emit('submit',this.formName)
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<style scoped>

</style>
```

```



为了节约短信费用，可以把verifications/views.py下的SmsCodeView里面的发送短信注释掉，只保留储存验证码到redis这段代码



##### 4.1.11 后端验证短信验证码



新建verifications/serializers.py

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from django_redis import get_redis_connection

class CheckSmsCodeSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    '''
    校验短信验证码
    '''
    # 通过get_serializer返回一个序列化器对象，restframework会象对象里面的context属性补充三个数据
    # request, format(前端请求的数据格式),view(当前类视图对象本身), 这三个对象可以在定义序列化器时候使用
    # 我们的路径参数mobile放在view视图对象下面
    sms_code = serializers.CharField(label='短信验证码')

    def validate_sms_code(self, value):
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('verify_codes')
        # 获取手机号
        mobile = self.context['view'].kwargs['mobile']
        # 获取储存在redis中的短信验证码
        redis_sms_code = redis_conn.get('sms_%s' % mobile)

        if not redis_sms_code:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('无效的或者已过期的短信验证码')

        # 对比短信验证码
        if value != redis_sms_code.decode():
            raise serializers.ValidationError('短信验证码错误')

        return value


```



修改verifications/views.py

添加校验短信验证码

```
from .serializers import CheckSmsCodeSerializer

# 校验短信验证码
class CheckSmsCodeView(GenericAPIView):
    serializer_class = checkSmsCodeSerializer
    def get(self, request, mobile):
        serializer = self.get_serializer(data=request.query_params)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
        return Response({'message': '短信验证成功'}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
```



修改verifications/url.py

```
re_path(r'smscheck/(?P<mobile>1[3-9]\d{9})/$', views.CheckSmsCodeView.as_view()),
```

##### 4.1.12 封装后端生成短信验证码和发送验证短信

新建verifications/utils.py

```
from rest_framework import status, serializers
from django_redis import get_redis_connection
from captcha.image import ImageCaptcha

import random,string
import logging, json

logger = logging.getLogger('django')
from . import constants
from xiaofu.libs.sms_code import Sms
from xiaofu.libs.sms_constants import accId,appId,accToken

class CodeDeal():
    # media_detail 比如手机号13888889999 邮箱zs@qq.com等
    def __init__(self,connection_name, media_detail, media_type="sms"):
        self.connection_name = connection_name
        self.media_detail = media_detail
        self.media_type = media_type
        self._redis_conn = None
        self._connect()

	# 链接redis
    def _connect(self):
        self._redis_conn = get_redis_connection(self.connection_name)
    
    # 后端生成短信验证码并保存在redis库中
    def generate_code(self):
        # redis_conn = get_redis_connection(self.connection_name)

        # 检查验证码是否发送过于频繁
        verify_flag = self._redis_conn.get('%s_flag_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail))
        print('%s_flag_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail))
        print(verify_flag)
        if verify_flag is not None:
            detail_info = '发送%s验证码过于频繁' %constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC.get(self.media_type)
            raise serializers.ValidationError(detail_info)
        # 6位数随机验证码
        verify_code = '%6d' % random.randint(100000, 999999)

        # # 设置短信有效期
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, sms_code)
        # # 设置短信发送间隔
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_flag_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL,1)

        # 建立管道
        pl = self._redis_conn.pipeline()
        # 批量执行命令
        pl.setex('%s_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail), constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, verify_code)
        pl.setex('%s_flag_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail) , constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL, 1)
        # 执行管道命令
        pl.execute()

        return verify_code


    # 发送短信验证码
    def send_sms_code(self, sms_code):
        # 发送短信验证码
        sms_obj = Sms(accId, accToken, appId)
        sms_valid_time = int(constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE / 60)
        # sms_resp = json.loads(sms_obj.send_message(constants.SMS_TEMPLATE_ID,self.mobile, [sms_code, sms_valid_time]))

        sms_resp = send_sms.delay(self.media_detail, sms_code) # 通过delay方法异步执行
        print("sms_result:",sms_resp.state)  # 获取结果状态
        print(sms_resp.get()) # 获取返回的结果信息
        print(sms_resp.id)    # 获取任务id
        sms_result = json.loads(sms_resp.get())
        if sms_result.get('statusCode') != "000000":
            logger.error('手机号%s发送短信异常, 错误代码%s, 错误信息%s' % (self.media_detail,sms_result.get('statusCode'),sms_result.get('statusMsg')))
            
 # 根据前端传送过来的验证码code和后端redis储存的验证码code对比是否一致
    def verify_code(self, code):
        # redis_conn = get_redis_connection(self.connection_name)

        # 获取储存在redis中的验证码 e.g sms_13888889999
        redis_code = self._redis_conn.get('%s_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail))

        if not redis_code:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('%s验证码非法或者已过期' %constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC)

        # 对比短信验证码
        if code != redis_code.decode():
            raise serializers.ValidationError('%s验证码错误' %constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC)           
```



修改verifications/constants.py 添加

# 各种验证码说明
MEDIA_TYPE_DESC = {
    'sms': '短信',
    'email': '邮件',
    'captcha': '图片'
}

```



修改verifications.views.py下的SmsCodeView使用封装版

```
# 发送短信验证码
class SmsCodeView(GenericAPIView):
    def get(self, request, mobile):
        # 最终封装版
        sms_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', mobile)
        sms_code = sms_obj.generate_code()
        # sms_obj.send_sms_code(sms_code)
        return Response({'message':"发送短信验证码成功"},status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
```



修改verifications/serializers.py下的CheckSmsCodeSerializer

```
class checkSmsCodeSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    '''
    校验短信验证码
    '''
    # 通过get_serializer返回一个序列化器对象，restframework会象对象里面的context属性补充三个数据
    # request, format(前端请求的数据格式),view(当前类视图对象本身), 这三个对象可以在定义序列化器时候使用
    # 我们的路径参数mobile放在view视图对象下面
    sms_code = serializers.CharField(label='短信验证码')

    def validate_sms_code(self, value):
        mobile = self.context['view'].kwargs['mobile']
        sms_obj = CodeDeal("verify_codes", mobile)
        sms_obj.verify_code(value)
        return value
```

### 4.2 axios封装

##### 4.2.1 使用axios封装

新建utils/myAxios.js

```
// 封装axios请求，返回重新封装的数据格式
// 统一的错误处理

import axios from 'axios'
import errorHandle from "./errorHandler";

const instance = axios.create();
instance.defaults.baseURL = process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production' ? 'http://192.168.70.102:8000': 'http://domain.com'


instance.interceptors.request.use(config => {
    console.log('config:',config)
    return config;
}, error => {
    errorHandle(error)
    return Promise.reject(error);
});

instance.interceptors.response.use( res => {
    console.log('res is ', res)
    if (res.status >=200 && res.status<300) {
        return Promise.resolve(res.data);
    } else {
        return Promise.reject(res)
    }
}, error => {
    debugger
    errorHandle(error)
    return Promise.reject(error);
});

export default instance
```

新建utils/errorHandler.js

```
import { Message } from 'element-ui'
const errorHandle = (err) => {
    let error_msg = ''
    if(err.toString().indexOf('timeout')){
        console.log("超时啦",err)
    }
    
    if (err.response.data.detail) {
        error_msg = err.response.data.detail
        console.log(error_msg)
    }
    else if (err.response.data) {
        let err_obj = err.response.data
        for(let name in err_obj) {
            error_msg = err_obj[name].toString()
        }
    }
    else {
        error_msg = '服务器端错误，请检查日志'
    }

    Message.error({
        message: error_msg,
        closable: true
    });
}

export default errorHandle
```



新建src/api/Account.js

```
// 发送短信验证码
import axios from '@/utils/myAxios'

const sms = (mobile) => {
    return axios.get('/sms/' + mobile)
}

export { sms }
```

##### 4.2.2 axios封装成类

修改utils/myAxios.js 封装成类

```
// 封装axios请求，返回重新封装的数据格式
// 统一的错误处理

import axios from 'axios'
import config from '@/config'
import errorHandle from "./errorHandler";

class HttpRequest {
    constructor(baseUrl) {
        this.baseUrl = baseUrl
    }
    // 获取axios配置
    getInsideConfig() {
        const config = {
            baseURL: this.baseUrl,
            timeout: 10000
        }
        return config
    }
    // 设置拦截器
    interceptors (instance) {
        instance.interceptors.request.use(config => {
            console.log('config:',config)
            return config;
        }, error => {
            errorHandle(error)
            return Promise.reject(error);
        });

        instance.interceptors.response.use( res => {
            console.log('res is ', res)
            if (res.status >=200 && res.status<300) {
                return Promise.resolve(res.data);
            } else {
                return Promise.reject(res)
            }
        }, error => {
            debugger
            errorHandle(error)
            return Promise.reject(error);
        });
    }
    // 创建实例
    request (options) {
        const instance = axios.create()
        this.interceptors(instance)
        const newOptions = Object.assign(this.getInsideConfig(),options)
        console.log("newOptions:",newOptions)
        return instance.request(newOptions) // 等价于instance.request(newOptions)
    }

    get (url, params, config) {
        const options = Object.assign({
            method: 'get',
            url: url,
            params: params
        },config)
        return this.request(options)
    }
    post (url, data) {
        const options = Object.assign({
            method: 'post',
            url: url,
            data: data
        })
        return this.request(options)
    }
}

export default HttpRequest
```



新增utils/request.js

```
import HttpRequest from './myAxios'
import config from '@/config'
const baseUrl = process.env.NODE_ENV ==='development' ? config.baseUrl.dev : config.baseUrl.pro

const axios = new HttpRequest(baseUrl)

export default axios
```



修改api/Account.js

##### 4.2.4 检查手机号唯一性

后端修改

修改users/views.py

```
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from rest_framework.response import Response

from users.models import User

class CheckMobileView(APIView):
    """
    手机号是否唯一
    """
    def get(self, request, mobile):
        try:
            user = User.objects.get(mobile=mobile)
            if user:
                flag = False
        except:
            flag = True

        data = {
            'mobile': mobile,
            'flag': flag
        }

        return Response(data)

```



修改users/urls.py

```
from django.urls import path,include,re_path
from users import views


urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'check-mobile/(?P<mobile>1[3-9]\d{9})/$', views.CheckMobileView.as_view()),
]
```



修改外层urls.py 添加用户url

##### 4.2.5 通用唯一性

手机号，email，用户名都需要唯一性，编写统一的唯一性验证



修改users/models.py 添加如下方法

```
@classmethod
    def check_unique_user(self, filters):
        try:
            user = self.objects.get(**filters)
            if user:
                flag = False
        except:
            flag = True
        data = {
            'flag': flag
        }
        return data
```



修改users/views.py

注释CheckUniqueMobileView

添加如下内容

```

from .models import User
from rest_framework import status

# 根据传入的条件动态判断username或者email或者mobile是否唯一
# http://192.168.70.102:8000/check-unique-user/?username=zhangsan
{username: zhangsan}
class CheckUniqueUserView(APIView):
    def get(self, request):
        filters = {}
        for key, value in request.query_params.items():
            filters.update({key: request.query_params.get(key)})
        # 只能有一个条件判断比如username或者mobile等    
        if (len(filters) != 1):
            return Response({"detail": '非法判断条件'},status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        data = User.check_unique_user(filters)
        return Response(data)
```



修改users/urls.py添加路由

```
re_path(r'check-unique-user/$', views.CheckUniqueUserView.as_view()),
```

### 4.3 Celery 异步发送短信

##### 4.3.1 Celery架构说明图

![](水印pics\celery说明图.png)



##### 4.3.2 Celery异步发短信

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 ~]$ pip install Celery
```

项目celery的结构

![](水印pics\Celery结构.png)



在celery_tasks目录下新建config.py

```
broker_url = "redis://192.168.70.101/14"
result_backend = "redis://192.168.70.101/15"
```



在celery_tasks目录下新建main.py

```
from celery import Celery
import os
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'xiaofu.settings.dev')

# 起一个名字叫xiaofu
celery_app = Celery('xiaofu')

# 加载配置信息
celery_app.config_from_object('celery_tasks.config')

# 自动发现任务
celery_app.autodiscover_tasks(['celery_tasks.sms'])


```

在sms目录下移入sms_code.py

新建sms/sms_constants.py

```
accId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b5bb1001'
accToken = '153d19a...fb9ec22121435e7c6'
appId = '8aaf070878d419aa0178fc79b6b01007'

# 短信验证码有效期
SMS_CODE_EXPIRE = 300

# 短信发送间隔
SMS_CODE_INTERVAL = 60

# 短信模板ID
SMS_TEMPLATE_ID = 1
```



新建sms/tasks.py

```
from celery_tasks.main import celery_app

from .sms_code import Sms
from .sms_constants import *


# 使用装饰器装饰异步任务，保证celery识别任务
@celery_app.task(name='send_sms')
def send_sms(mobile, sms_code):
    sms_obj = Sms(accId, accToken, appId)
    sms_valid_time = int(SMS_CODE_EXPIRE / 60)
    sms_resp = sms_obj.send_message(SMS_TEMPLATE_ID, mobile, [sms_code, sms_valid_time])
    return sms_resp


```

启动celery 注意启动路径

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 xiaofu]$ ls
celery_tasks  logs  manage.py  scripts  utils  xiaofu
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 xiaofu]$ pwd
/home/apps/project/xiaofu
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 xiaofu]$ celery -A celery_tasks.main worker -l info
 
```



修改verifications/utils.py

```
   from celery_tasks.sms.tasks import send_sms
   
   def send_sms_code(self, sms_code):
        # 发送短信验证码
        sms_resp = send_sms.delay(self.media_detail, sms_code) # 通过delay方法异步执行
        sms_result = json.loads(sms_resp.get())
        if sms_result.get('statusCode') != "000000":
            logger.error('手机号%s发送短信异常, 错误代码%s, 错误信息%s' % (self.media_detail,sms_result.get('statusCode'),sms_result.get('statusMsg')))


```







### 4.4  注册信息填写

##### 4.4.1 前端界面

前端新建Account/Register/RegInfo.vue

```
<template>
    <div class="info-form">
        <el-form ref="formValidate" label-position="right" :model="formValidate" label-width="100px" :rules="ruleValidate">
            <el-form-item label="用户名" prop="username">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.username" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请输入用户名"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="设置密码" prop="password">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.password" type="password" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请输入密码"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="确认密码" prop="password_confirm">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.password_confirm" type="password" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请再次输入密码"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="邮箱验证" prop="email">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.email" clearable size="large"  placeholder="请输入邮箱"></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="邮箱验证码" prop="email_code">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.email_code" size="large"  placeholder="请输入邮箱验证码">
                    <el-button style="width:150px" :disabled="email_disable" ref="email_button" slot="append" @click="getEmailCode">{{email_code_tip}}</el-button>
                </el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-button type="danger"  style="width: 100%"  @click="Register('formValidate')">立即注册</el-button>
        </el-form>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    export default {
        name: "Info",
        data() {
            // 验证密码
            let check_pass = (rule, value, callback) => {
                if (value === '') {
                    callback(new Error('请再次输入密码'));
                } else if (value !== this.formValidate.password) {
                    callback(new Error('两次输入密码不一致!'));
                } else {
                    callback();
                }
            };

            // 验证邮箱格式
            let check_email = (rule, value, callback) => {
                let mailReg = /^([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+@([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+(.[a-zA-Z0-9_-])+/
                if (!value) {
                    return callback(new Error('邮箱不能为空'))
                }
                if (mailReg.test(value)) {
                    callback()
                } else {
                    callback(new Error('请输入正确的邮箱格式'))
                }
            }

            // 验证邮箱验证码
            let check_email_code = (rule, value, callback) => {
                if (!Number.isInteger(+value)) {
                    callback(new Error('请输入6位数字值'))
                } else {
                    callback()
                }
            }


            return {
                formValidate: {
                    username: '',
                    password: '',
                    password_confirm: '',
                    email: '',
                    email_code: ''
                },
                ruleValidate: {
                    username: [
                        { required: true, message: '用户名不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', max: 30, message: '用户名最大长度为30', trigger: 'blur' }

                    ],
                    password: [
                        { required: true, message: '密码不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', min: 6, message: '密码最小为6位', trigger: 'blur' }
                    ],
                    password_confirm: [
                        { required: true, message: '确认密码不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { validator: check_pass, trigger: 'blur' }
                    ],
                    email: [
                        { required: true, message: '邮箱不能为空啦', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { validator: check_email, trigger: 'blur' }
                    ],
                    email_code: [
                        { required: true, message: '邮箱验证码不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', min: 6, max:6, message: '邮箱验证码是6位数字', trigger: 'blur' },
                      
                    ]
                },
                email_code_tip: '获取验证码',
                email_disable: ''
            }
        },
        methods: {
            getEmailCode() {
                console.log('hahah')
            },
            Register() {
                console.log("reg")
            }
        }

    }
</script>

<style lang="stylus" scoped>
    .info-form
        width 80%
</style>
```



![](水印pics\填写账号信息.png)





##### 4.4.2 检查用户名和email唯一性前端

import { checkUniqueUser } from '@/api/Account'

            // 检查用户名唯一性
            let check_unique_username = (rule, value, callback) => {
                checkUniqueUser({"username": value}).then(res => {
                    if (res.flag === false) {
                        callback(new Error('该用户名已经被注册') )
                    } else {
                        callback()
                    }
                })
            }
            
            // 检查email唯一性
            let check_unique_email = (rule, value, callback) => {
                checkUniqueUser({"email": value}).then(res => {
                    if (res.flag === false) {
                        callback(new Error('该email已经被注册') )
                    } else {
                        callback()
                    }
                })
            }

username: [
                        { required: true, message: '用户名不能为空', trigger: 'blur' },

                        { validator: check_unique_username, trigger: 'blur' },

                    ],
                    
                    
                    
                    email: [
                        { required: true, message: '邮箱不能为空啦', trigger: 'blur' },

##### 4.4.3 Celery获取邮箱验证码

修改settings/dev.py

ebgeg'  # 邮箱授权时获得的密码，非注册登录密码

celery_tasks下面新建email包

新建email/tasks.py

```
from django.core.mail import send_mail
from django.conf import settings
from celery_tasks.main import celery_app

# 读取django项目的配置
import os
if not os.getenv('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE'):
    os.environ["DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE"] = "xiaofu.settings.dev"



@celery_app.task(name='send_email_code')
def send_email_code(to, email_code):
    #send_mail('标题','普通邮件正文','发件人','收件人列表','富文本邮件正文(html)')
    subject = '小福商城邮箱验证码'
    html_message = '<p>亲爱的用户您好！</p>' \
                   '<p>您的邮箱验证码为：%s 。请在5分钟内输入有效.</p>' \
                   %(email_code)
    try:
        send_mail(subject, '', settings.EMAIL_FROM, [to], html_message=html_message)
    except Exception as e:
        pass

# 发送邮箱验证码测试
send_email_code(settings.TEST_EMAIL,'555666')

```





测试成功

修改celery_tasks下的main.py

添加注册任务celery_tasks.email

```
from celery import Celery
import os
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'xiaofu.settings.dev')

# 起一个名字叫小福
celery_app = Celery('xiaofu')

# 加载配置信息
celery_app.config_from_object('celery_tasks.config')

# 自动发现任务
celery_app.autodiscover_tasks(['celery_tasks.sms','celery_tasks.email'])
```



##### 4.4.4 发送邮箱验证码后端

```
    def send_email_code(self, email_code):
        # 发送短信验证码
        email_resp = send_email_code.delay(self.media_detail,email_code)
        print("email_result:", email_resp)  # 获取结果状态
```





修改verifications/views.py

发送email 验证码

```
# GET email/(?P<email>([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+@([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+.([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+)/$
# 发送email 验证码
class EmailCodeView(GenericAPIView):
    def get(self, request, email):
        email_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', email, media_type='email')
        email_code = email_obj.generate_code()
        email_obj.send_email_code(email_code)
        return Response({'message':"发送邮箱验证码成功"},status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
```

```
    import { email_send } from '@/api/Account'
	
	// 获取邮箱验证码
            getEmailCode() {
                this.$refs['formValidate'].validateField('email', errMsg => {
                    if (!errMsg) {
                        let second = 10
                        this.email_code_tip = second + '秒'
                        let t =setInterval(() => {
                            if (second === 1) {
                                clearInterval(t)
                                this.email_disable = false
                                this.email_code_tip = '获取邮箱验证码'
                            }
                            else {
                                second -=1
                                this.email_code_tip = second + '秒'
                                this.email_disable=true
                            }
                        },1000)
                        let email = this.formValidate.email
                        email_send(email).then(res => {
                            console.log("res:", res)
                        })

                    } else {
                        return false
                    }
                })

            },

##### 4.4.6 数据有效期的分类设置



修改verifications/constants.py

添加超时的基类以及短信和Email继承类

```
class CodeTTLBase():
    EXPIRE = 5 * 60
    INTERVAL = 60

class SmsCodeTTL(CodeTTLBase):
    pass

class EmailCodeTTL(CodeTTLBase):
    EXPIRE = 5 * 80
```



修改verifications/utils.py

根据url中的media_type动态获取对应的发送类型的有效期时间

```
 		
 		# 根据url传入的media_type拼接类名
        class_name = self.media_type.capitalize() + 'CodeTTL'
        # 引入constants包, 如果不加fromlist=('constants',) 返回的模块是verifications,如果加上了的话，返回的模块是constants模块
        obj = __import__('verifications.constants',fromlist=('constants',))
        # 动态获取类, eg SmsCodeTTL
        class_obj=getattr(obj, class_name)
        # 使用getattr获取类属性
        expire = getattr(class_obj,'EXPIRE', 60 * 5)
```





```
    def generate_code(self):
        # 检查短信是否发送过于频繁
        # sms_flag_13888889999
        verfify_flag = self._redis_conn.get('%s_flag_%s' %(self.media_type, self.media_detail))
        if verfify_flag is not None:
            detail_info = '发送%s验证码过于频繁' %constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC.get(self.media_type)
            raise serializers.ValidationError(detail_info)

        # 生成6位的短信验证码
        sms_code = '%6d' % random.randint(100000, 999999)

        # 设置短信的有效期
        # {sms_13888889999: '123456'}
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_EXPIRE, sms_code)
        # 设置短信的发送间隔
        # redis_conn.setex('sms_flag_%s' %mobile, constants.SMS_CODE_INTERVAL, 1)
        
        
        pl = self._redis_conn.pipeline()
        # 根据url传入的media_type拼接类名
        class_name = self.media_type.capitalize() + 'CodeTTL'
        # 引入constants包
        obj = __import__('verifications.constants',fromlist=('constants',))
        # 动态获取类, eg SmsCodeTTL
        class_obj=getattr(obj, class_name)
        # 使用getattr获取类属性
        expire = getattr(class_obj,'EXPIRE', 60 * 5)
        interval = getattr(class_obj,'INTERVAL', 60)
        pl.setex('%s_%s' % (self.media_type, self.media_detail), expire, sms_code)
        pl.setex('%s_flag_%s' % (self.media_type, self.media_detail), interval, 1)
        pl.execute()
        
        return sms_code
```



封装成方法

修改verifications/utils.py

添加getExpireAndInterval方法

```
    def getExpireAndInterval(self, path, module):
        # obj = __import__('verifications.constants', fromlist=('constants',))
        obj = __import__(path, fromlist=(module,))
        class_name = self.media_type.capitalize() + 'CodeTTL'
        class_obj = getattr(obj, class_name)
        expire = getattr(class_obj, 'EXPIRE', 60 * 5)
        interval = getattr(class_obj, 'INTERVAL', 60)
        return expire, interval

```

修改generate_code方法

使用

```
expire, interval = self.getExpireAndInterval('verifications.constants','constants')
```





##### 4.4.7 动态显示邮箱或者手机等验证码报错信息

修改verifications/constants

添加

```
# 各种验证码说明
MEDIA_TYPE_DESC = {
    'sms': '短信验证码',
    'email': '邮件验证码',
    'captcha': '图片验证码'
}
```

修改verifications/utils.py

修改verify_code方法，可以动态显示邮箱或者手机等验证码报错信息

```
    def verify_code(self, code):
        # 获取储存在redis中的短信验证码
        redis_code = self._redis_conn.get('%s_%s' % (self.media_type, self.media_detail) )

        # 验证码是否无效或者过期
        if not redis_code:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('%s验证码非法或者已过期' % constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC.get(self.media_type))

        # 对比验证码
        if code != redis_code.decode():
            raise serializers.ValidationError('%s验证码错误' % constants.MEDIA_TYPE_DESC.get(self.media_type))
```



### 4.5 注册实现

##### 4.5.1 后端接口

**请求方式**： POST `/users/`

| 参数名           | 类型 | 是否必须 | 说明       |
| ---------------- | ---- | -------- | ---------- |
| username         | str  | 是       | 用户名     |
| password         | str  | 是       | 密码       |
| password_confirm | str  | 是       | 确认密码   |
| email            | str  | 是       | 邮箱       |
| email_code       | str  | 是       | 邮箱验证码 |
| mobile           | str  | 是       | 手机号     |
| uuid             | str  | 是       | 唯一的uuid |

**返回数据**： JSON

```json
{
    "id": 1,
    "username": "forever",
    "mobile": "13888889999",
    "email": "forever@qq.com"
}
```



新建users/serializers.py

```
from rest_framework import serializers

import re

from verifications.utils import CodeDeal
from users.models import User



class UserCreateSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    """
    创建用户序列化器
    """
    password_confirm = serializers.CharField(label='确认密码', write_only=True)
    email_code = serializers.CharField(label='邮箱验证码', write_only=True)

    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ('id', 'username', 'password', 'password_confirm','email', 'email_code', 'mobile')
        extra_kwargs = {
            'username': {
                'min_length': 3,
                'max_length': 18,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                    'max_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                }
            },
            'password': {
                'write_only': True,
                'min_length': 6,
                'max_length': 20,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '密码不能小于6位',
                }
            }
        }

    def validate_mobile(self, value):
        """验证手机号"""
        if not re.match(r'^1[3-9]\d{9}$', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('手机号码格式错误')
        return value

    def validate_email(self, value):
        """验证邮箱"""
        if not re.match(r'([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+@([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+.([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('邮箱格式错误')
        return value


    def validate(self, data):
        # 判断两次密码
        if data['password'] != data['password_confirm']:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('两次输入的密码不一致')

       # 判断邮箱验证码
        email = data['email']
        code_email_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes',email, "email")
        code_email_obj.verify_code(data['email_code'])

        return data

    def create(self, validated_data):
        """
        创建用户
        """
        # 移除数据库模型类中不存在的属性
        del validated_data['password_confirm']
        del validated_data['email_code']
        user = super().create(validated_data)

        # 调用django的认证系统加密密码
        user.set_password(validated_data['password'])
        user.save()

        return user
```



修改users/views.py

使用UserViewSet来创建用户

```
from .serializers import UserCreateSerializer

class UserViewSet(ModelViewSet):
    queryset = User.objects.all()
    
    def get_serializer_class(self):
        if self.action == 'create':
            return UserCreateSerializer
        return UserCreateSerializer //不加这个return会报错， 后续需要修改，    
```



修改users/urls.py添加创建用户路由

```
 from rest_framework import routers
 
 router = routers.SimpleRouter()
 router.register(r'users', views.UserViewSet)

urlpatterns += router.urls

```

![](水印pics\创建用户成功.png)

此处的问题: 手机号可以随意填写



问题解决

修改verifications/utils.py

添加uuid:mobile 注册时候redis保存手机号

```
    def reg_code(self):
        expire, interval = self.getExpireAndInterval('verifications.constants','constants')
        uid = str(uuid.uuid1())
        pl = self._redis_conn.pipeline()
        pl.setex('reg_%s' % (uid), expire, self.media_detail)
        pl.execute()
        return uid
```



修改verifications/views.py

添加一个flag_info来判断是否是注册步骤

当serializer验证完后, 用redis将手机号绑定一个uuid并返回

```
# 校验短信验证码
class CheckSmsCodeView(GenericAPIView):
    serializer_class = checkSmsCodeSerializer
    def get(self, request, mobile):
        serializer = self.get_serializer(data=request.query_params)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

       # http://192.168.70.102:8000/smscheck/13888885555/?sms_code=184095&flag=reg
        flag_info = request.query_params.get('flag')
        if flag_info:
            if flag_info == 'reg':
                sms_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', mobile)
                uuid = sms_obj.reg_code()
                return Response({'detail': '短信验证成功',"uuid":uuid, "mobile": mobile }, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)

        return Response({'detail': '短信验证成功'}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)

```



redis储存的手机号和uuid关系

```
127.0.0.1:6379[2]> get reg_93edfef6-280d-11ec-9b76-000c29b201a3
"13888889999"
```



修改verifications/constants.py

```
# 各种验证码说明
MEDIA_TYPE_DESC = {
    'sms': '短信验证码',
    'email': '邮件验证码',
    'captcha': '图片验证码',
    'reg': '注册手机号'
}
```



修改users/serializers.py

添加判断手机号是否有效的验证(通过uuid和手机号绑定来验证)

需要添加uuid字段

validate里面判断手机号是否有效

```
from rest_framework import serializers

import re

from verifications.utils import CodeDeal
from .models import User



class UserCreateSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    """
    创建用户序列化器
    """
    password_confirm = serializers.CharField(label='确认密码', write_only=True)
    email_code = serializers.CharField(label='邮箱验证码', write_only=True)
    uuid = serializers.CharField(label='UUID', write_only=True)

    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ('id', 'username', 'password', 'password_confirm','email', 'email_code', 'mobile', 'uuid')
        extra_kwargs = {
            'username': {
                'min_length': 3,
                'max_length': 18,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                    'max_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                }
            },
            'password': {
                'write_only': True,
                'min_length': 6,
                'max_length': 20,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '密码不能小于6位',
                }
            }
        }

    def validate_mobile(self, value):
        """验证手机号"""
        if not re.match(r'^1[3-9]\d{9}$', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('手机号码格式错误')
        return value

    def validate_email(self, value):
        """验证邮箱"""
        if not re.match(r'([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+@([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+.([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('邮箱格式错误')
        return value


    def validate(self, data):
        # 判断两次密码
        if data['password'] != data['password_confirm']:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('两次输入的密码不一致')

        # 判断邮箱验证码
        email = data['email']
        code_email_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes',email, "email")
        code_email_obj.verify_code(data['email_code'])

        # 判断手机号是否有效
        uuid = data['uuid']
        mobile = data['mobile']
        code_reg_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', uuid, "reg")
        code_reg_obj.verify_code(mobile)

        return data

    def create(self, validated_data):
        """
        创建用户
        """
        # 移除数据库模型类中不存在的属性
        del validated_data['password_confirm']
        del validated_data['email_code']
        del validated_data['uuid']
        user = super().create(validated_data)

        # 调用django的认证系统加密密码
        user.set_password(validated_data['password'])
        user.save()

        return user
```



##### 4.5.2 前端实现用户注册

修改Register/Sms.vue

在checkSms中添加SAVE_MOBILE用来保存uuid以及mobile

在mapMutations添加SAVE_MOBILE,  params变量添加"flag":"reg"

```
handleSubmit (name) { // 提交验证
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let mobile = this.formValidate.phone
                        let input_sms_code = this.formValidate.sms_code
                        let params = {"sms_code": input_sms_code, "flag":"reg"}

                        checkSms(mobile,params).then(res => {
                            this.SET_SIGN_UP_SETP(1);
                            this.SAVE_MOBILE({"uuid":res.uuid, "mobile": res.mobile})
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            that.sms_disable = false
                           
                        })
                    } else {
                        this.$message.error({
                            message: '请填写正确的信息',
                            closable: true
                        });
                    }
                });
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_SIGN_UP_SETP','SAVE_MOBILE']),

```





修改store/index.js添加userInfo

```
const state = {
  signUpStep: 0, // 登陆步骤
  userInfo: {
    mobile: '',   // 手机号
  },
  uuid: ''      // uuid
}


```



修改store/mutations.js

```
// 注册时候保留手机号
export const SAVE_MOBILE = (state, data) => {
    state.userInfo.mobile = data.mobile;
    state.uuid = data.uuid
};

```

修改Register/RegInfo.vue

添加Register方法，并且import userReg

```
import { checkUsername, checkEmail, email, userReg } from '@/api/login'
import {mapMutations, mapState} from 'vuex';


Register(name) {
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "username": this.formValidate.username,
                            "password": this.formValidate.password,
                            "password_confirm": this.formValidate.password_confirm,
                            "email": this.formValidate.email,
                            "email_code": this.formValidate.email_code,
                            "mobile": this.userInfo.mobile,
                            "uuid": this.uuid
                        }
                        userReg(post_data).then(res => {
                        	localStorage.clear()
                            this.SET_SIGN_UP_SETP(3);
                        }).catch(function(err){

                        })
                    }
                })
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_SIGN_UP_SETP'])
            
            
            
            
            computed: {
            ...mapState(['userInfo','uuid'])
        },

```



修改Register/Done.vue, 10秒钟后跳转首页

```
<template>
    <div class="done">
        <div class="info">
            <span>注册成功</span>
            <span class="sec">{{count}}</span>
            <span>秒后跳转</span>
            <router-link to="/" class="home">首页</router-link>
        </div>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    export default {
        name: "Done",
        data() {
            return {
                count: ''
            }
        },
        methods: {
            goHome () {
                let second = 10;
                this.count = second
                let t = setInterval(() => {
                    if (second === 1) { // 倒计时即将结束
                        clearInterval(t); // 停止回调函数的执行
                        this.$router.push('/')
                    } else { // 正在倒计时
                        second -= 1; // num = num - 1;
                        this.count = second
                    }
                }, 1000)
            }
        },

        mounted() {
            this.goHome()
        }
    }
</script>

<style lang="stylus" scoped>
    .done
        display flex
        justify-content center
        align-items center
        width 90%
        height 90%
        background-color: #fff
        .sec
            color red
        .info
            font-size 24px
        .home
            color red

</style>

```

修改settings/dev.py

添加jwt用户认证以及JWT 扩展配置

```
REST_FRAMEWORK = {
    # 指定DRF框架异常处理函数
    'EXCEPTION_HANDLER': 'xiaofu.utils.exceptions.exception_handler',

    # 用户认证
    'DEFAULT_AUTHENTICATION_CLASSES': (
        # 引入JWT 认证机制
        'rest_framework_jwt.authentication.JSONWebTokenAuthentication',
       
    ),
}

# JWT 扩展配置
JWT_AUTH = {
    # jwt token有效时间
    'JWT_EXPIRATION_DELTA': datetime.timedelta(days=10),
}
```





修改users/serializers.py

 添加token = serializers.CharField(label='Token', read_only=True)

在fields中添加token字段，

最后在create方法中给user对象生成一个token

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from django_redis import get_redis_connection

import re

from users.models import User



class CreateUserSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    """
    创建用户序列化器
    """
    password_confirm = serializers.CharField(label='确认密码', write_only=True)
    email_code = serializers.CharField(label='邮箱验证码', write_only=True)
    uuid = serializers.CharField(label='UUID', write_only=True)
    token = serializers.CharField(label='Token', read_only=True)

    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ('id', 'username', 'password', 'password_confirm','email', 'email_code', 'mobile','uuid', 'token')
        extra_kwargs = {
            'username': {
                'min_length': 3,
                'max_length': 18,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                    'max_length': '仅允许3-18个字符的用户名',
                }
            },
            'password': {
                'write_only': True,
                'min_length': 6,
                'max_length': 20,
                'error_messages': {
                    'min_length': '密码不能小于6位',
                }
            }
        }

    def validate_mobile(self, value):
        """验证手机号"""
        if not re.match(r'^1[3-9]\d{9}$', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('手机号码格式错误')
        return value

    def validate_email(self, value):
        """验证邮箱"""
        if not re.match(r'([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+@([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+.([a-zA-Z0-9_-])+', value):
            raise serializers.ValidationError('邮箱格式错误')
        return value


    def validate(self, data):
        # 判断两次密码
        if data['password'] != data['password_confirm']:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('两次输入的密码不一致')

        # 判断邮箱验证码
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('verify_codes')
        email = data['email']
        email_code = redis_conn.get('email_%s' % email)
        if email_code is None:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('无效的邮箱验证码')
        if data['email_code'] != email_code.decode():
            raise serializers.ValidationError('邮箱验证码有误')

        # 判断手机号是否有效
        uid = data['uuid']
        print("uid",uid)
        mobile = data['mobile']
        redis_mobile = redis_conn.get(uid)
        if redis_mobile is None:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('无效的手机号')
        if mobile != redis_mobile.decode():
            raise serializers.ValidationError('手机号有误')


        return data

    def create(self, validated_data):
        """
        创建用户
        """
        # 移除数据库模型类中不存在的属性
        del validated_data['password_confirm']
        del validated_data['email_code']
        del validated_data['uuid']
        user = super().create(validated_data)

        # 调用django的认证系统加密密码
        user.set_password(validated_data['password'])
        user.save()

        # 用户注册成功后就直接让用户处于登录状态
        # 服务器会签发一个jwt token，保存用户身份信息
        from rest_framework_jwt.settings import api_settings

        jwt_payload_handler = api_settings.JWT_PAYLOAD_HANDLER
        jwt_encode_handler = api_settings.JWT_ENCODE_HANDLER

        # 生成载荷信息(payload)
        payload = jwt_payload_handler(user)
        # 生成jwt token
        token = jwt_encode_handler(payload)

        # 给user对象增加一个属性token，保存jwt token信息
        user.token = token

        return user
```



注册成功后返回前端的数据

```
{
    "id":20,
    "username":"qhqh",
    "email":"hq@qq.com",
    "mobile":"13888889999",

##### 4.5.4 前端保存用户信息

修改Register/RegInfo.vue



```
 Register(name) {
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "username": this.formValidate.username,
                            "password": this.formValidate.password,
                            "password_confirm": this.formValidate.password_confirm,
                            "email": this.formValidate.email,
                            "email_code": this.formValidate.email_code,
                            "mobile": this.userInfo.mobile,
                            "uuid": this.userInfo.uuid
                        }
                        userReg(post_data).then(res => {
                            localStorage.clear()	    				this.SET_USER_INFO({"userid":res.id,"username":res.username,"email":res.email,"mobile":res.mobile})
                            this.SET_IS_LOGIN(true)
                            this.SET_TOKEN(res.token)
                            this.SET_SIGN_UP_SETP(2);
                        }).catch(function(err){

                        })
                    }
                })
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_SIGN_UP_SETP','SET_USER_INFO','SET_IS_LOGIN','SET_TOKEN'])
```

```
// 设置token
export const SET_TOKEN = (state, value) => {
    state.token = value
    localStorage.setItem('token',value)
};

// 设置用户信息
export const SET_USER_INFO = (state, value) => {
    state.userInfo = value
    localStorage.setItem('userInfo',JSON.stringify(value))
};

// 设置是否登陆
export const SET_IS_LOGIN = (state, value) => {
    state.isLogin = value
}
```

##### 4.5.5  登录路由优化（全局路由守卫）

修改router/index.js 

添加全局路由守卫，在需要登陆的页面没登陆的话跳转到 Login页面

```
import Login from '../views/Login'

import store from '@/store'

{path: '/login', name: 'login', component: Login},



router.beforeEach((to,from,next) => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token')
  if (token !== '' && token !== null) {
    store.commit('SET_TOKEN', token)
    store.commit('SET_IS_LOGIN', true)
  }
  if (to.matched.some(record => record.meta.requiresAuth)) {
    const isLogin = store.state.isLogin
    if (isLogin) {
      next()
    } else {
      next('/login')
    }
  } else {
    next()
  }
})
```



新建views/Login.vue

```
<template>
    <div>
        login
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    export default {
        name: "Login"
    }
</script>

<style scoped>

</style>
```



可以使用register路由添加

meta: { requiresAuth: true}

来测试路由是否会跳转





##### 4.5.6 登录安全机制优化（jwt过期后处理逻辑）

```
npm install -S jsonwebtoken
npm install moment
```



修改router/index.js

判断token是否过期，如果过期则清空localstorage

```
router.beforeEach((to,from,next) => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token')
  if (token !== '' && token !== null) {
    const payload = jwt.decode(token)
    if (moment().isBefore(moment(payload.exp * 1000))) {
      store.commit('SET_TOKEN', token)
      store.commit('SET_IS_LOGIN', true)
    } else {
      console.log("clear")
      localStorage.clear()
      store.commit('SET_IS_LOGIN', false)
    }

  }

  if (to.matched.some(record => record.meta.requiresAuth)) {
    const isLogin = store.state.isLogin
    if (isLogin) {
      next()
    } else {
      next('/login')
    }
  } else {
    next()
  }
})
```



修改后端token有效期位5秒

```
    'JWT_EXPIRATION_DELTA': datetime.timedelta(seconds=5),
```



给"/"路由添加requiresAuth: true进行测试,

当注册完成10秒后需要跳转首页，由于5秒钟的时候localStorage被清空，所以isLogin为false，因此会跳转到/login路由

```
  {
    path: '/',
    name: 'Home',
    component: Home,
    meta: { requiresAuth: true}
  },
```

这个时候会有一个报错信息

![](水印pics\路由redirected报错信息.png)



再次修改router/index.js

在router.beforeEach前添加如下代码解决

```
const originalPush = VueRouter.prototype.push
VueRouter.prototype.push = function push(location, onResolve, onReject) {
  if (onResolve || onReject) return originalPush.call(this, location, onResolve, onReject)
  return originalPush.call(this, location).catch(err => err)
}
```





# 5 前端vuex使用modules

新建store/modules/user.js

```
const user = {
    state: {
        signUpStep: 0, // 登陆步骤
        isLogin: false,
        token:'',
        uuid: '',      // uuid
        userInfo: {
            username: '',
            userid: '',
            email: '',
            mobile: '',   // 手机号
        },
    },
    mutations: {
        SET_SIGN_UP_SETP:  (state, step) => {
            state.signUpStep = step;
        },
        SAVE_MOBILE: (state, data) => {
            state.userInfo.mobile = data.mobile;
            state.uuid = data.uuid
        },
        SET_TOKEN: (state, value) => {
            state.token = value
            localStorage.setItem('token',value)
        },
        SET_USER_INFO: (state, value) => {
            state.userInfo = value
            localStorage.setItem('userInfo',JSON.stringify(value))
        },
        SET_IS_LOGIN: (state, value) => {
            state.isLogin = value
        }

    },
    actions: {  },
    getters: {  }
}

export default user
```

# 6 登陆

### 6.1 为jwt补充userid和username

https://jpadilla.github.io/django-rest-framework-jwt/

In your `urls.py` add the following URL route to enable obtaining a token via a POST included the user's username and password.

```
from rest_framework_jwt.views import obtain_jwt_token
#...

urlpatterns = [
    '',
    # ...

    url(r'^api-token-auth/', obtain_jwt_token),
]
```



修改uses/url.spy

获取jwt token

```
   from rest_framework_jwt.views import obtain_jwt_token

   
   re_path(r'^login/$', obtain_jwt_token),
```



![](水印pics\jwt token.png)



**自定义JWT_RESPONSE_PAYLOAD**

JWT_RESPONSE_PAYLOAD_HANDLER

Responsible for controlling the response data returned after login or refresh. Override to return a custom response such as including the serialized representation of the User.

Defaults to return the JWT token.

Example:

```
def jwt_response_payload_handler(token, user=None, request=None):
    return {
        'token': token,
        'user': UserSerializer(user, context={'request': request}).data
    }
```

Default is `{'token': token}`





新建users/utils.py

获取token以及userid和username

```
def jwt_response_payload_handler(token, user=None, request=None):
    return {
        'token': token,
        'userid': user.id,
        'username': user.username,
        'email': user.email,
        'mobile': user.mobile
    }
```





修改settings/dev.py

指定JWT 扩展登录视图生成响应数据调用函数

```
# JWT 扩展配置
JWT_AUTH = {
    # jwt token有效时间
    'JWT_EXPIRATION_DELTA': datetime.timedelta(days=1),

    # 指定JWT 扩展登录视图生成响应数据调用函数
    'JWT_RESPONSE_PAYLOAD_HANDLER': 'users.utils.jwt_response_payload_handler'
}
```



![](水印pics\jwt token2.png)







### 6.2 用户自定义登陆后端

修改users/utils.py

自定义用户认证，可以用手机号，用户名或者邮箱登陆

```
from django.contrib.auth.backends import ModelBackend
from django.db.models import Q
from rest_framework import exceptions

# 自定义用户认证，可以用手机号，用户名或者邮箱登陆
class customUserLogin(ModelBackend):
    def authenticate(self, request, username=None, password=None, **kwargs):
        try:
            # 手机号，用户名或者邮箱登陆进行查验用户是否存在
            user = User.objects.get(Q(username=username) | Q(mobile=username) | Q(email=username))
        except User.DoesNotExist:
            return None
        # 如果用户存在并且密码检查通过则返回用户
        if (user and user.check_password(password)):
            return user
        else:
            raise exceptions.AuthenticationFailed("用户名密码错误")
```





修改settings/dev.py

添加自定义Django的认证系统

```
# 自定义Django的认证系统
AUTHENTICATION_BACKENDS = [
    'users.utils.customUserLogin'
]
```

### 6.4 后端验证码实现

```
pip install captcha
```



获取图片的url

```
http://192.168.70.102:8000/captcha/9bf4dfd6-66dc-11ec-9f89-000c29cac2d5
```



修改verifications/utils.py

产生图片验证码以及验证码文字

```
from captcha.image import ImageCaptcha

import random,string

def gen_captcha_text_and_image(width=20, height=30,save=None):
    image = ImageCaptcha(width=width, height=height)
    characters = string.digits + string.ascii_lowercase
    captcha_text = ''.join([random.choice(characters) for j in range(4)])
    captcha_image = image.generate(captcha_text)
    return captcha_text, captcha_image

if __name__ == "__main__":
    captcha_text, captcha_image = gen_captcha_text_and_image()
    # print(captcha_text,captcha)
```





修改verifications/utils.py

原来的 def reg_code(self）

修改为def set_uuid_coded(self, type, uuid): 根据传入的type来获取对应的超时时间, 传入uuid

```
    def set_uuid_code(self, type, uuid):
        expire, interval = self.getExpireAndInterval('verifications.constants','constants')
        pl = self._redis_conn.pipeline()
        pl.setex('%s_%s' %(type, uuid), expire, self.media_detail)
        pl.execute()
```







修改verifications/views.py

添加CaptchaView 返回图片验证码

```
from .utils import gen_captcha_text_and_image
from django.http.response import HttpResponse

class CaptchaView(GenericAPIView):
    # 生成图片验证码并且返回图片给前端,image_code_id是前端传过来的uuid
    def get(self, request, uuid):
        text, image = gen_captcha_text_and_image(100, 55)
        captcha_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', text, "captcha")
        uid = captcha_obj.set_uuid_code('captcha', uuid)
        
        # redis_conn = get_redis_connection("verify_codes")
        # redis_conn.setex("captcha_%s" % uuid, 300, text)  # 在redis中保存{img_'uuid':图片验证码4位字符串}
        return HttpResponse(image, content_type="images/png")
```



在verifications/urls.py添加图形验证码路由

```
# 图形验证码
re_path(r'^captcha/(?P<uuid>[\w-]+)/$', views.CaptchaView.as_view()),
```



------





修改verifications/views.py

在class CheckSmsCodeView(GenericAPIView) 中uuid = sms_obj.reg_code('reg', uid)需要传入参数reg, uid

```
        import uuid
        
        if flag_info:
            if flag_info == 'reg':
                sms_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', mobile)
                uid = str(uuid.uuid1())
                sms_obj.set_uuid_code('reg', uid)
                return Response({'detail': '短信验证成功', "uuid": uid, "mobile": mobile}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)


```



### 6.5 前端实现验证码

```



修改Login/LoginInfo.vue

在methods 添加get_captcha 获取验证码方法

mounted中使用this.get_captcha()

```
import config from '@/config'

const baseUrl = process.env.NODE_ENV ==='development' ? config.baseUrl.dev : config.baseUrl.pro

methods: {
            get_captcha() {
                let uuid = this.$uuid.v4()
                this.image_code_url = baseUrl + '/captcha/' + uuid + '/';
            },
        },
        mounted() {
            this.get_captcha()
        }
```



![](水印pics\登陆带验证码.png)



### 6.6 重写JSONWebTokenAPIView实现用户登陆

由于还需要验证图片验证码，所以我们需要重写obtain_jwt_token

```
obtain_jwt_token = ObtainJSONWebToken.as_view()
```



```
class ObtainJSONWebToken(JSONWebTokenAPIView):
    """
    API View that receives a POST with a user's username and password.

    Returns a JSON Web Token that can be used for authenticated requests.
    """
    serializer_class = JSONWebTokenSerializer
```



修改verifications.utils.py 下的CodeDeal	

添加方法delete_code删除验证码

```
    def delete_code(self):
        # 获取储存在redis中的验证码 e.g sms_13888889999
        redis_code = self._redis_conn.delete('%s_%s' % (self.media_type, self.media_detail))

```





修改users/serializers.py  新建CaptchaSerializer，处理图片验证码

修改users/serializers.py  新建LoginSerializer， 继承JSONWebTokenSerializer,CaptchaSerializer

```
from rest_framework_jwt.serializers import JSONWebTokenSerializer


class CaptchaSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    captcha = serializers.CharField(label='验证码', write_only=True)
    uuid = serializers.CharField(label='uuid', write_only=True)

    def validate_captcha(self, value):
        # 从get传过来的参数中获取uuid
        uuid = self.context['request'].data.get("uuid")
        if uuid is None:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('验证码uuid为空')
        captcha_obj = CodeDeal("verify_codes", uuid, 'captcha')
        captcha_obj.verify_code(value)
        captcha_obj.delete_code('captcha', uuid)

        return value

class LoginSerializer(JSONWebTokenSerializer,CaptchaSerializer):
    def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        """
        Dynamically add the USERNAME_FIELD to self.fields.
        """
        super(LoginSerializer, self).__init__(*args, **kwargs)
```





修改users/views.py

添加LoginView继承JSONWebTokenAPIView

```
from rest_framework_jwt.views import JSONWebTokenAPIView

class LoginView(JSONWebTokenAPIView):
    serializer_class = LoginSerializer
```



修改users/urls.py

```
   re_path(r'^login2/$', obtain_jwt_token),
   re_path(r'^login/$', views.LoginView.as_view()),
```





![](水印pics\后端登陆带图片验证码.png)







### 6.7 前端实现用户登录



修改api/Account.js

添加用户登录并且export

```
// 用户登录
const userLogin = (data) => {
    return axios.post('/login/', data)
}





export { sms, email, checkMobile, checkSms, checkUsername, checkEmail, userReg, userLogin }
```



修改Login/LoginInfo.vue

data添加参数uuid, methods get_captcha里面this.uuid = uuid

添加Login登录，登录成功后跳转首页

```
    import { userLogin } from '@/api/Account'


get_captcha() {
                let uuid = this.$uuid.v4()
                this.uuid = uuid
                this.image_code_url = baseUrl + '/captcha/' + uuid + '/'
            }


Login(name) {
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "username": this.formValidate.username,
                            "password": this.formValidate.password,
                            "captcha": this.formValidate.captcha,
                            "uuid": this.uuid,
                        }
                        userLogin(post_data).then(res => {
                            console.log(res)
                            localStorage.clear()
                        this.SET_USER_INFO({"userid":res.userid,"username":res.username,"email":res.email,"mobile":res.mobile})
                            this.SET_IS_LOGIN(true)
                            this.SET_TOKEN(res.token)
                            this.$router.push('/')
                        }).catch(function(err){

                        })
                    }
                })
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_USER_INFO','SET_IS_LOGIN','SET_TOKEN'])
```
