### 7-4 根据用户是否登录显示不同信息

修改common/MainHeader.vue

如果用户没登录显示“登录/注册”, 如果用户登录了则显示用户名

```
				<div class="register fl">	
					<template v-if="!isShow">
                        <router-link :to="{name: 'login'}">登陆</router-link>
                        <span>/</span>
                        <router-link :to="{name: 'register'}">注册</router-link>
                    </template>
                    <template v-else>
                        <div class="userinfo">
                            <span class="username">{{username}}</span>
                        </div>
                    </template>
                </div>
                
                
      computed: {
            isShow() {
                return this.isLogin
            },
            username() {
               return this.userInfo.username
           },
            ...mapState({'userInfo': state=>state.user.userInfo, 'isLogin': state=>state.user.isLogin})
      }       
      
      
      
      
      // css中添加
      .register
            .title
                margin-right: 16px;
            .userinfo
                display inline-block
                .username
                    font-size: 14px;
                    color: #ccc;
```





### 7-5 保持登录状态

安装包

```
npm install moment
npm install jsonwebtoken
```



修改router/index.js

添加router.beforeEach判断token是否超时，

```
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken'
import moment from 'moment'
import store from '@/store'

router.beforeEach((to,from,next) => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token')
  if (token !== '' && token !== null) {
    const payload = jwt.decode(token)
    if (moment().isBefore(moment(payload.exp * 1000))) {
      store.commit('SET_TOKEN', token)
      store.commit('SET_IS_LOGIN', true)
      next()
    } else {
      localStorage.clear()
      store.commit('SET_IS_LOGIN', false)
      next()
    }
  } else {
    next()
  }
})
```





修改store/modules/user.js

通过Localstorage获取用户信息

```
let defaultUserInfo = {}

try {
    if (localStorage.userInfo) {
        defaultUserInfo = JSON.parse(localStorage.userInfo)
        console.log("defaultUserInfo", defaultUserInfo)
    }
} catch (e) {
    defaultUserInfo = {
        username: '',
        userid: '',
        email: '',
        mobile: '',   // 手机号
    }
}

state: {
        	userInfo: defaultUserInfo,
        }
```



### 7-6 退出登录

修改common/MainHeader.vue

当鼠标移动到用户名的时候弹出下拉用户信息框

通过methods show和hide 来显示和隐藏

mouseover和mouseleave必须作用在div标签下扩大范围

```
<template v-else>
                        <div class="userinfo" @mouseover="show" @mouseleave="hide">
                            <span class="username">
                                {{username}}
                            </span>

                            <div class="profile-nav-submenu" :class=showUserClass>
                                <div class="profile-nav-submenu-panel">
                                    <div class="profile-nav-user-wrapper">
                                        <a href="" class="profile-nav-user-avatar">
                                            <img src="../../assets/pics/jerry.webp" alt="">
                                        </a>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="profile-nav-user-info">
                                        <p class="profile-nav-user-operate">
                                            <router-link :to="{}" class="user-operate">账号管理</router-link>
                                            <span class="sep">|</span>
                                            <a href="javascript:void(0)" class="user-operate" @click="logout">退出</a>
                                        </p>
                                        <p class="credit">
                                            积分: 200
                                        </p>
                                        <p class="level_info">
                                            普通会员
                                        </p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </template>
                    
           
           data() {
            return {
                hoverCtrl: {},
                showUserClass: {
                    'showuser': true
                }
            }
        },
           
           
           methods: {
            show() {
                // 鼠标移入头像时候显示操作菜单
                clearTimeout(this.hoverCtrl)
                this.hoverCtrl = setTimeout(()=> {
                    this.showUserClass.showuser = false
                },200)
            },
            hide() {
                // 鼠标移出头像时候隐藏操作菜单
                clearTimeout(this.hoverCtrl)
                this.hoverCtrl = setTimeout(()=> {
                    this.showUserClass.showuser = true
                },200)
            }
        },
                    
                    
<style lang="stylus" scoped>                    
          .register
            .title
                margin-right: 16px
            .userinfo
                display inline-block
            .showuser
                display none
            .profile-nav-submenu
                z-index 999
                position relative
                .profile-nav-submenu-panel
                    position: absolute;
                    left: 0px;
                    top: -10px;
                    padding: 8px
                    line-height: normal;
                    border: 1px
                    solid #EEEEEE;
                    background: #FFF;
                    width 248px
                    border-radius 10px
                    .profile-nav-user-wrapper
                        float: left;
                        margin 0 10px
                        width: 62px
                        height: 62px
                        padding: 10px
                        box-sizing: content-box;
                        .profile-nav-user-avatar
                            display: block;
                            overflow: hidden;
                            border: 1px
                            solid #fff;
                            border-radius: 50%;
                            img
                                display block
                                height 62px
                                width 62px
                    .profile-nav-user-info
                        height: 80px
                        overflow: hidden;
                    .profile-nav-user-operate
                        text-align right
                        .sep
                            padding 0 5px
                            color: #ddd;
                    .user-operate,.credit,.level_info
                        font-size 12px
                        color: #3c3c3c
                        height 20px
                        line-height 20px
                    .credit,.level_info
                        margin-top 5px
                        font-size 12px
</style>
```





![](水印pics\用户信息弹框.png)





修改main.js 引入MessageBox

```
import { Steps, Step, Button, Message, Input, Form, FormItem, MessageBox  } from 'element-ui';
Vue.prototype.$messagebox  = MessageBox
```



修改MainHeader.vue

添加logout方法，退出登录后需要清空localstorage

```
logout() {
                console.log("yaya")
                this.$messagebox.confirm('是否退出登录', {
                    confirmButtonText: '确定',
                    cancelButtonText: '取消',
                    type: 'warning'
                }).then(() => {
                    this.$message({
                        type: 'success',
                        message: '成功退出登录!'
                    });
                    this.SET_TOKEN('')
                    this.SET_IS_LOGIN(false)
                    this.SET_USER_INFO({})
                    localStorage.clear()
                }).catch(() => {
                    this.$message({
                        type: 'success',
                        message: '退出登录失败!'
                    });
                });
            },
            
            ...mapMutations(['SET_TOKEN','SET_IS_LOGIN','SET_USER_INFO'])
```

const router = new VueRouter({

})

第二种高亮显示方法

<template>

    <div class="side-container">
        <h2 class="title active">账户管理</h2>
        <div class="sub_nav">
            <ul>
                <li v-for="(item, index) in menu" class="menu_item" >

                        {{item.name}}
                    </router-link>
                </li>

    </div>

        name: "sideBar",
        data () {
            return {
                menu: [
                    {"name":'安全设置', "link":"safe", activeClass: 'act-class'},
                    {"name":'个人资料', "link":"profile", activeClass: 'act-class'},
                    {"name":'收获地址', "link":"address", activeClass: 'act-class'}
                ]
            }
        }
    }
</script>

### 8.3 路由登录验证

修改router/index.js

使用meta定义需要验证的路由

通过判断某个路由是否需要登录来跳转到对应页面

```
{ path: '/account',
    component: Account,
    name: 'account',
    meta: { requiresAuth: true},
    children: [
      { path: 'safe', name: 'safe', component: Safe, meta: { requiresAuth: true} },
      { path: 'profile', name: 'profile', component: Profile, meta: { requiresAuth: true} },
      { path: 'address', name: 'address', component: Addr, meta: { requiresAuth: true}}
    ]
  },


if (to.meta.requiresAuth) {
    const isLogin = store.state.user.isLogin
    if (isLogin) {
      next()
    } else {
      // 判断需要跳转的路由是否是login，如果是则直接跳转
      if (to.path === '/login') {
        next()
      } else {
        // 判断需要跳转的路由是否是login，如果不是则记录下query，方便登录后跳转到对应页面
        next({
          path:"/login",
          query: { next: to.fullPath}
        })
      }

    }
  } else {
    console.log(to)
    next()
  }
```



修改Login/LoginInfo.vue

在Login 方法中判断是否有下一跳next的参数，如果有则登录后跳转到对应路由

```
let next_page = decodeURIComponent(this.$route.query.next || '/')
                            this.$router.push({path: next_page})
```



```
Login(name) {
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "username": this.formValidate.username,
                            "password": this.formValidate.password,
                            "captcha": this.formValidate.captcha,
                            "uuid": this.uuid,
                        }
                        userLogin(post_data).then(res => {
                            localStorage.clear()
                            this.SET_USER_INFO({"userid":res.id,"username":res.username,"email":res.email,"mobile":res.mobile})
                            this.SET_IS_LOGIN(true)
                            this.SET_TOKEN(res.token)
                            let next_page = decodeURIComponent(this.$route.query.next || '/')
                            this.$router.push({path: next_page})
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            console.log(err.response)
                        })
                    }
                })
            },
```

新建utils/qiniu_storage.py

```
# https://portal.qiniu.com/user/key 获取AccessKey/SecretKey
AK = 'h0RtLtxGBQ4ICPzRIMSVzN1fpA2F...'
SK = 'M3Wm...'

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
# flake8: noqa
from qiniu import Auth, put_file, etag
import qiniu.config

from xiaofu.utils.qiuniu_constants import AK,SK


def upload(localfile):
    #需要填写你的 Access Key 和 Secret Key
    access_key = AK
    secret_key = SK
    #构建鉴权对象
    q = Auth(access_key, secret_key)
    #要上传的空间，这个是空间名
    bucket_name = 'forevercool'
    #上传后保存的文件名，设置为None让七牛为我们生成文件名
    key = None
    #生成上传 Token，可以指定过期时间等
    token = q.upload_token(bucket_name, key, 3600000)
    #要上传文件的本地路径
    # localfile = './sync/bbb.jpg'
    ret, info = put_file(token, key, localfile, version='v2')
    # ret, info = put_data(token,key,file_data)
    print("ret: ",ret)
    print("info: ",info)
    return ret['key']

if __name__ == "__main__":
    upload('/home/apps/project/xiaofu/img/logo.png')

```

在utils下新建file_related.py

check_image_file 检查是否是图片

```
import imghdr
def check_image_file(file_name):
    """
    检查是否是图片
    :param value:
    :return:
    """
    try:
        file_type = imghdr.what(file_name)
    except Exception:
        raise ValueError('非法的图片')
    else:
        if not file_type:
            raise ValueError('非法的图片')
        else:
            return file_name
```

        model = User
        fields = ('id', 'avatar_file_name')

```
    from django.conf import settings
    from rest_framework.decorators import action
    
    from xiaofu.utils.qiniu_storage import upload
	from xiaofu.utils.file_related import check_image_file
   
   
   @action(methods=['post'], detail=True, url_path='update-user-avatar', url_name='update-user-avatar', name='update-user-avatar')
    def update_avatar(self,request,pk):
        instance = self.get_object()
        img = request.FILES['avatar_image']
        check_image_file(img)
        file_name = upload(img)
        data = {}
        data['avatar_file_name'] = file_name

        serializer = self.get_serializer(instance=instance,data=data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
        self.perform_update(serializer)

		# 头像图片的url
        avatar_url = settings.QINIU_DOMAIN + file_name

        return Response({"detail": "更新成功","avatar_url": avatar_url })
        
        
        def get_serializer_class(self):
            if self.action == 'create':
                return CreateUserSerializer
            if self.action == 'update_avatar':
                return UserAvatarSerializer
   			return CreateUserSerializer

后端修改users/utils.py，登录时候补充上用户头像

jwt_response_payload_handler 添加avatar_file_name

需要判断user.avatar_file_name是否为空，不为空显示用户头像，否则显示为空

```
from django.conf import settings

def jwt_response_payload_handler(token, user=None, request=None):
    if (user.avatar_file_name):
        avatar_file_name = settings.QINIU_DOMAIN + user.avatar_file_name
    else:
        avatar_file_name = ""
    return {
        'token': token,
        'userid': user.id,
        'username': user.username,
        'email': user.email,
        'mobile': user.mobile,
        'avatar_file_name': avatar_file_name
    }

```

```
	import { mapState, mapMutations } from "vuex";
		
		
            data() {
                return {
                    formValidate: {
                        nickname: '',
                        realname: '',
                        sex:''
                    },
                    action_url: "",
                    imageUrl: '',
                }
            },
			methods: {
            	handleAvatarSuccess(res, file) {

                },
                beforeAvatarUpload(file) {
                    const isJPG = file.type === 'image/jpeg';
                    const isLt1M = file.size / 1024 / 1024 < 1;

                    if (!isJPG) {
                        this.$message.error('上传头像图片只能是 JPG 格式!');
                    }
                    if (!isLt1M) {
                        this.$message.error('上传头像图片大小不能超过 1MB!');
                    }
                    return isJPG && isLt1M;
                }
            }
		
		created() {
            		this.imageUrl = this.userinfo.avatar_url
            	},
        computed: {
            ...mapState({'userinfo': state=>state.user.userInfo})
        },

##### 8.7.2 头像更新

修改Account/UserDetail/Profile.vue

```
action_url 需要在created时候填充好
```



在el_upload里面添加

```
name="avatar_image"
```



处理成功上传文件后把imageUrl复制为后端的avatar_url

```
handleAvatarSuccess(res, file) {
                this.imageUrl = res.avatar_url
            },
```

问题，刷新页面后头像会消失

```

        methods: {
            handleAvatarSuccess(res, file) {
                this.imageUrl = res.avatar_url
            },
           
        },
        created() {
            this.imageUrl = this.userinfo.avatar_url
            this.action_url = "http://192.168.70.102:8000/users/" + this.userinfo.userid +"/update-user-avatar/"
        },
        computed: {
            ...mapState({'userinfo': state=>state.user.userInfo})
        },
    }
</script>

```



解决办法 通过mutation解决

添加SET_AVATAR

```
SET_AVATAR: (state, value) => {
            state.userInfo.avatar_url = value
            
            let user_info = JSON.parse(localStorage.userInfo)
            user_info.avatar_url=value
            localStorage.setItem('userInfo',JSON.stringify(user_info))
            
        },
```





修改Account/Profile.vue

```
在handleAvatarSuccess下添加this.SET_AVATAR(res.avatar_url)

methods中添加...mapMutations(['SET_AVATAR'])
```



```
methods: {
            handleAvatarSuccess(res, file) {
                // this.imageUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file.raw);
                console.log(res)
                this.imageUrl = res.avatar_url
                this.SET_AVATAR(res.avatar_url)
            },
            
            ...mapMutations(['SET_AVATAR'])
        },
        
```

**权限的添加**

修改users/views.py

引入IsAuthenticated 添加get_permissions方法

```
    from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated
    
    def get_permissions(self):
        if self.action == 'update' or self.action == 'update_avatar':
            return (IsAuthenticated(),)
        return []
```



上面一步只能保证用户是否登录，而登录后的用户还能修改其他用户的信息

因此需要继承BasePermission，重写has_object_permission方法

新建utils/perm.py

```
from rest_framework import permissions

class IsOwner(permissions.BasePermission):
    def has_object_permission(self, request, view, obj):
        return obj == request.user
```



修改users/views.py

引入IsOwner

在UserViewSet下的get_permissions里添加IsOwner

```
from utils.perm import IsOwner

    def get_permissions(self):
        if self.action == 'update' or self.action == 'update_avatar':
            return (IsAuthenticated(),IsOwner())
        return []
```





### 8.9 昵称 姓名 性别修改前端

**页面显示用户信息**

后端python在UserViewSet中get_permissions中retrieve方法也需要认证

在get_serializer_class中默认返回UserInfoSerializer

```
    def get_permissions(self):
        if self.action == 'update' or self.action == 'update_avatar' or self.action == 'retrieve':
            return (IsAuthenticated(), IsOwner(),)
        return []
        
        
        
    def get_serializer_class(self):
        if self.action == 'create':
            return UserCreateSerializer
        if self.action == 'update_avatar':
            return UserAvatarSerializer
        if self.action == 'update':
            return UserInfoSerializer
        return UserInfoSerializer
```

export const TOKEN_KEY = 'token'

export const getToken = () => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem(TOKEN_KEY)
    if (token) return token
    else return false
}

# 9 用户地址



### 9.1 用户地址增删改查后端

##### 9.1.1 创建model

新建utils/models.py

```
from django.db import models

class BaseModel(models.Model):
    """为模型类补充字段"""

    create_time = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True, verbose_name="创建时间")
    update_time = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True, verbose_name="更新时间")

    class Meta:
        abstract = True  # 说明是抽象模型类, 用于继承使用，数据库迁移时不会创建BaseModel的表

```



修改users/models.py

添加Address

```
from xiaofu.utils.models import BaseModel

class Address(BaseModel):
    """用户地址"""
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name='addresses', verbose_name='用户')
    receiver = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='收货人')
    province = models.CharField(max_length=20,  verbose_name='省')
    city = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='市')
    district = models.CharField(max_length=20,  verbose_name='区')
    address_detail = models.CharField(max_length=80, verbose_name='地址')
    tel = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='手机/电话')
    is_deleted = models.BooleanField(default=False, verbose_name='逻辑删除')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '用户地址'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name
        ordering = ['-update_time']
```



修改users/models.py  User类下添加default_address

```
default_address = models.ForeignKey('Address', related_name='user_default_address', null=True, blank=True,
                                        on_delete=models.SET_NULL, verbose_name='默认地址')
```



##### 9.1.2 创建AddressSerializer

新建Users/constants.py

```
MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM = 20
```



修改users/serializers.py添加AddressSerializer

```
from .constants import MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM

class AddressSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Address
        fields = '__all__'
        
    # 需要判断发送过来的用户是否为当前登录的用户，如果不是则报错    
    def validate_user(self, value):
        user = self.context['request'].user
        if user.username == value.username:
            return value
        else:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('必须使用当前登录用户创建地址')
            
    def validate(self, attrs):
        count = self.context['request'].user.addresses.filter(is_deleted=False).count()
        if count >= MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('保存地址数已经达到上线%s条' %MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM)
        return attrs    
```



##### 9.1.3 地址的增删改查

修改users/urls.py

添加用户地址路由

```
router.register(r'user-address', views.UserAddressViewSet)
```



修改users/views.py添加UserAddressViewSet

重写create方法，地址添加成功后判断用户是否有默认地址，没有默认地址则给用户添加默认地址

```
from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated


class UserAddressViewSet(ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Address.objects.all().filter(is_deleted=False)
    serializer_class = AddressSerializer
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def create(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
        data = request.data.copy()
        data.update({"user": request.user.id})
        serializer = self.get_serializer(data=data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
        self.perform_create(serializer)
        headers = self.get_success_headers(serializer.data)
        
        # 前端请求中如果default_address如果为True,则把当前创建的地址设置为默认地址
        if data.get('default_address'):
            request.user.default_address = serializer.instance
            request.user.save()

        # 如果用户没有默认地址，则设置一个默认地址
        if not request.user.default_address:
            created_address_id = serializer.data.get('id')
            request.user.default_address_id = created_address_id
            request.user.save()

        return Response(serializer.data, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED, headers=headers)
```









新建utils/perm.py

判断对象所属的用户是否是当前的请求用户

```
from rest_framework import permissions

class hasPermission(permissions.BasePermission):
    def has_object_permission(self, request, view, obj):
        return obj.user == request.user
```



修改users/views.py 添加权限不然当前登录用户可以访问其他用户的地址

引入IsOwner 并且permission_classes里面添加IsOwner

```
from utils.perm import hasPermission

permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated, hasPermission]
```





修改users/views.py

在UserAddressViewSet中 添加如下方法

```
from .constants import MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM

	def get_queryset(self):
        return self.request.user.addresses.filter(is_deleted=False)
        
    def list(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
        """
        地址列表
        """
        queryset = self.get_queryset()
        serializer = self.get_serializer(queryset, many=True)
        user = self.request.user
        return Response({
            'default_address_id': user.default_address_id,
            'limit': MAX_USER_ADDRESS_NUM,
            'addresses': serializer.data,
        })
        
    def update(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
        data = request.data.copy()
        data.update({"user": request.user.id})
        instance = self.get_object()
        serializer = self.get_serializer(instance, data=data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
        self.perform_update(serializer)

        if data.get('default_address'):
            request.user.default_address = serializer.instance
            request.user.save()

        return Response(serializer.data)    

    def destroy(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
        """
        处理删除
        """
        addr_instance = self.get_object()
        # 进行逻辑删除
        addr_instance.is_deleted = True
        addr_instance.save()

        return Response({'detail': '删除成功'},status=status.HTTP_204_NO_CONTENT)

    # put /address/pk/change-default-addr/
    @action(methods=['put'], detail=True, url_path='change-default-addr', url_name='change-default-addr',)
    def changeDefaultAddr(self, request, pk=None):
        """
        设置默认地址
        """
        address = self.get_object()
        print(address.user_id, address.id, address.address_detail)
        request.user.default_address = address
        request.user.save()
        return Response({'detail': '设置默认地址成功'}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)

```

##### 9.2.2 获取地址列表

修改api/Account.js

请求后端获取地址列表，需要在header中添加token

```
import { getToken } from "@/utils/token";
import axios from '@/utils/request'

const getAddressList = () => {
    return axios.get('/user-address/', '',{
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}

export { getAddressList }
```



修改Account/UserDetail/Addr.vue

created时候获取地址列表

```
    import { getAddressList } from '@/api/Account'
    
    _getAddrList() {
                getAddressList().then(res => {
                    this.tableData = res.addresses
                    this.default_address_id = res.default_address_id
                    this.left_table_amount = res.limit - this.tableData.length
                })
            }
    
    created() {
            this._getAddrList()
        }
```



修改基础页面信息

```
// 已经保存了{{tableData.length}}条地址，还能保存{{left_table_amount}}条

<div class="title addr_count">
    <span>已经保存了{{tableData.length}}条地址，还能保存{{left_table_amount}}条</span>
</div>


// 省市区显示
<el-table-column
	label="所在地区"
	width="180"
>
    <template slot-scope="scope">
        {{scope.row.province}} {{scope.row.city}} {{scope.row.district}}
    </template>
</el-table-column>


// 默认地址显示
<el-table-column
	label=""
	width="90"
>
	<template slot-scope="scope">
    	<span type="text" size="medium" v-if="scope.row.id==default_address_id" class="def_addr">默认地址</span>
        	<el-button type="text" size="medium" v-else>设为默认</el-button>
    </template>
</el-table-column>
```

##### 9.2.3 保存地址

修改api/Account.js

添加createAddr接口

```
const createAddr = (params) => {
    return axios.post('/user-address/', params,{
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}


export { createAddr }
```





地址创建后需要reset并且重新请求下地址列表

```
 # 如果设置默认地址，则需要传递信息到后端
 if ( this.formValidate.default_address == true) {
                            post_data['default_address'] = true
                        }
```

修改 Account/UserDetail/Addr.vue

添加saveAddr方法

```
    import { createAddr } from "@/api/Account";

			
			saveAddr(name) {
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "receiver": this.formValidate.receiver,
                            "province": this.formValidate.province,
                            "city": this.formValidate.city,
                            "district": this.formValidate.district,
                            "address_detail": this.formValidate.address_detail,
                            "tel": this.formValidate.tel,
                        }
                        if ( this.formValidate.default_address == true) {
                            post_data['default_address'] = true
                        }

                        createAddr(post_data).then(res => {
                            this.reset(name)
                            this._getAddrList()
                            this.$message.success({
                                message: '添加地址成功',
                                closable: true
                            });
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            this.$message.error({
                                message: '添加错误，请查看日志信息',
                                closable: true
                            });
                        })
                    }
                })
            },
            reset(name) {
                this.formValidate.province = ''
                this.formValidate.city = ''
                this.formValidate.district = ''
                this.$refs[name].resetFields()
            },
```



##### 9.2.4 直接设置默认地址

修改api/account.js

添加changeDefaultAddr

```
const changeDefaultAddr = (id) => {
    return axios.put('/user-address/'+ id +'/change-default-addr/','',{
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}
export { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr }
```



修改Account/Addr.vue

设为默认setDefaultAddr(scope.row.id)

引入changeDefaultAddr

添加方法setDefaultAddr

```
<el-button type="text" size="medium" v-else @click="setDefaultAddr(scope.row.id)">设为默认</el-button>

import { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr } from '@/api/account'

setDefaultAddr(id) {
                changeDefaultAddr(id).then(res => {
                    this._getAddrList()
                })
            },
```



##### 9.2.5 删除地址

修改utils/myAxios.js

添加delete方法

```
    delete (url, data, config) {
        const options = Object.assign({
            method: 'delete',
            url: url,
            data: data
        }, config)
        return this.request(options)
    }
```



修改api/account.js

添加deleteAddr

```
const deleteAddr = (id) => {
    return axios.delete('/user-address/'+ id ,'',{
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}
export { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr, deleteAddr }
```



修改Account/Addr.vue

点击删除delAddr(scope.row.id)

引入deleteAddr

添加方法delAddr

```
    <el-button type="text" size="medium" @click="delAddr(scope.row.id)">删除</el-button>
    
    import { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr, deleteAddr } from '@/api/account'
    
			delAddr(id) {
                console.log(id)
                deleteAddr(id).then(res => {
                    console.log(res)
                    this._getAddrList()
                })
            }
```



##### 9.2.6 更新地址

修改account.js 添加updateAddr

```
const updateAddr = (id,data) => {
    return axios.put('/user-address/'+ id + '/',data,{
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}

export { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr, deleteAddr, updateAddr }
```



修改Addr.vue

在data中添加action: 'createAddr'，通过action 来调用创建地址或者更新地址，添加formValidate.addr_id

添加方法modifyAddr，点击后会把当前的信息发到页面的form表单里面



```
<el-button type="text" size="medium" @click="modifyAddr(scope.row)">修改</el-button>


import { getAddressList, createAddress, changeDefaultAddr, deleteAddr, updateAddr } from '@/api/account'

formValidate: {
                    addr_id: '',

                },
                
action: 'createAddr'





if (this.action === 'createAddr') {
	createAddress(post_data).then(res => {
        this.reset(name)
        this._getAddrList()
        this.$message.success({
            message: '添加地址成功',
            closable: true
    	});
    }).catch(function(err){
        this.$message.error({
        message: '添加错误，请查看日志信息',
        closable: true
        });
    })
} else {
   updateAddr(this.formValidate.addr_id, post_data).then(res => {
       this.reset(name)
       this.action = 'createAddr'
       this._getAddrList()
       this.$message.success({
           message: '修改地址成功',
           closable: true
   		});
   }).catch(function(err){
       this.action = 'createAddr'
       this.$message.error({
           message: '修改错误，请查看日志信息',
           closable: true
       });
   })
}



modifyAddr(data) {
	this.action = 'updateAddr'
    this.formValidate.addr_id = data.id
    this.formValidate.province = data.province
    this.formValidate.city = data.city
    this.formValidate.district = data.district
    this.formValidate.receiver = data.receiver
    this.formValidate.tel = data.tel
    this.formValidate.address_detail = data.address_detail

    if (data.id === this.default_address_id) {
    	this.formValidate.default_address = true
    } else {
    	this.formValidate.default_address = false
    }
}
```

### 10.1 后端创建goods应用

创建goods app

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ ls
__init__.py  users  verifications
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py startapp goods

```

修改settings/dev.py

添加goods

```
INSTALLED_APPS = [
    'goods'
]
```



good/models.py

```
from django.db import models
from xiaofu.utils.models import BaseModel
# Create your models here.
# 商品三级分类
class GoodsCategory(BaseModel):
    """
    商品类别
    """
    name = models.CharField(max_length=12, verbose_name='商品类别名称')
    code = models.CharField(default="", max_length=30, verbose_name="类别code", help_text="类别code")
    parent = models.ForeignKey('self', null=True, blank=True, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='父类别')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '商品类别'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return self.name



# 左侧导航菜单显示的类别
class LeftMenuCategory(BaseModel):
    """
    左侧商品分类
    """
    category_group_id = models.IntegerField(verbose_name='分类组号')
    category = models.ForeignKey(GoodsCategory, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='顶级商品类别')
    sequence = models.IntegerField(verbose_name='组内顺序')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '左侧导航菜单类别'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return self.category.name

```

迁移

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py makemigrations
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py migrate

```





### 10.2 后端获取三级类别

新建goods/views.py



```
from django.shortcuts import render
from collections import OrderedDict
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from .models import LeftMenuCategory
from rest_framework.response import Response

class GetMenu(APIView):
    def get(self, request):
        categories = OrderedDict()
        top_category = LeftMenuCategory.objects.order_by('category_group_id', 'sequence')
        for left_menu in top_category:
            group_id = left_menu.category_group_id  # 当前组id

            if group_id not in categories:
                categories[group_id] = {'top_category': [], 'sub_cats': []}

            cat1 = left_menu.category  # 顶级类别

            # 追加当前顶级类别
            categories[group_id]['top_category'].append({
                'id': cat1.id,
                'name': cat1.name,
            })
            # 构建当前类别的子类别
            for cat2 in cat1.goodscategory_set.all():
                cat2.sub_cats = []
                for cat3 in cat2.goodscategory_set.all():
                    cat2.sub_cats.append({"id":cat3.id,"name":cat3.name})
                categories[group_id]   ['sub_cats'].append({"id":cat2.id,"name":cat2.name,"sub_cats": cat2.sub_cats})
        return Response(categories)


```

三级类别案例

		data() {

                menu: {},

        },

# centos下安装所需的软件包。yum-utils 提供了 yum-config-manager ，并且 device mapper 存储驱动程序需要 device-mapper-persistent-data 和 lvm2。

sudo yum install -y yum-utils \
  device-mapper-persistent-data \
  lvm2
  
  
  
  sudo yum-config-manager \
    --add-repo \
    http://mirrors.aliyun.com/docker-ce/linux/centos/docker-ce.repo
    
    
    
   # 安装最新版本的 Docker Engine-Community 和 containerd，
    sudo yum install docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io
    
    
    # 安装docker
    sudo yum install docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io
    
    # 查看版本
    docker -v
```





### 10.5 docker 拉取fastdfs

https://www.jianshu.com/p/d7e687967209

https://segmentfault.com/a/1190000018251300





```
# 拉去镜像
[apps@centos1 ~]$ sudo docker image pull delron/fastdfs

# 建立tracker以及storage目录
[apps@centos1 ~]$ sudo mkdir -p /var/fdfs/tracker
[apps@centos1 ~]$ sudo mkdir -p /var/fdfs/storage


# 启动tracker
[apps@centos1 ~]$ sudo docker run -dit --name tracker --network=host -v /var/fdfs/tracker:/var/fdfs delron/fastdfs tracker

# 启动storage 注意修改ip
[apps@centos1 ~]$ sudo docker run -dit --name storage --network=host -e TRACKER_SERVER=192.168.70.102:22122 -v /var/fdfs/storage:/var/fdfs delron/fastdfs storage


# 如果无法重新运行，可以删除/var/fdfs/storage/data目录下的fdfs_storaged.pid 文件，然后重新运行storage。
```

新建utils/fastdfs/client.conf 配置文件

```
# connect timeout in seconds
# default value is 30s
connect_timeout=30

# network timeout in seconds
# default value is 30s
network_timeout=60

# the base path to store log files
base_path=/home/apps/project/xiaofu/logs

# tracker_server can ocur more than once, and tracker_server format is
#  "host:port", host can be hostname or ip address
tracker_server=192.168.70.102:22122

#standard log level as syslog, case insensitive, value list:
### emerg for emergency
### alert
### crit for critical
### error
### warn for warning
### notice
### info
### debug
log_level=info

# if use connection pool
# default value is false
# since V4.05
use_connection_pool = false

# connections whose the idle time exceeds this time will be closed
# unit: second
# default value is 3600
# since V4.05
connection_pool_max_idle_time = 3600

# if load FastDFS parameters from tracker server
# since V4.05
# default value is false
load_fdfs_parameters_from_tracker=false

# if use storage ID instead of IP address
# same as tracker.conf
# valid only when load_fdfs_parameters_from_tracker is false
# default value is false
# since V4.05
use_storage_id = false

# specify storage ids filename, can use relative or absolute path
# same as tracker.conf
# valid only when load_fdfs_parameters_from_tracker is false
# since V4.05
storage_ids_filename = storage_ids.conf


#HTTP settings
http.tracker_server_port=80



```

### 10.7 自定义django文件存储

Django自带文件存储系统，默认文件存储在本地，本项目中我们需要将文件保存到FastDFS服务器上，所以需要自定义文件存储系统。

需要添加装饰器`django.utils.deconstruct.deconstructible`



修改setting/dev.py

添加FDFS的配置，自定义文件存储类

```
# FDFS配置
FDFS_CLIENT_CONF = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, 'utils/fastdfs/client.conf')
FDFS_URL = 'http://192.168.70.102:8888/'

# 指定Django系统使用的文件存储类
DEFAULT_FILE_STORAGE = 'xiaofu.utils.fastdfs.fdfs_storage.FDFSStorage'
```





新建utils/fastdfs/fdfs_storage.py

继承django storage，重写save, exists, url方法

```
# 自定义文件存储类
from django.conf import settings
from django.core.files.storage import Storage
from django.utils.deconstruct import deconstructible
from fdfs_client.client import Fdfs_client


@deconstructible
class FDFSStorage(Storage):
    """FDFS文件存储类"""
    def __init__(self, base_url=None, client_conf=None):
        """
        初始化
        base_url: 构造图片完整路径的使用，图片服务器的域名
        client_conf: FastDFS客户端配置文件路径
        """
        if base_url is None:
            base_url = settings.FDFS_URL

        self.base_url = base_url

        if client_conf is None:
            client_conf = settings.FDFS_CLIENT_CONF

        self.client_conf = client_conf

    def _save(self, name, content):
        """
        name: 上传文件的名称: logo.png
        content: 上传文件内容的File对象，通过content.read()获取上传文件内容
        """
        # 将文件上传到FDFS系统
        client = Fdfs_client(self.client_conf)

        res = client.upload_by_buffer(content.read())

        # 判断上传是否成功
        if res.get('Status') != 'Upload successed.':
            raise Exception('上传文件到FDFS失败')

        # 获取文件id
        file_id = res.get('Remote file_id')

        return file_id

    def exists(self, name):
        """
        用户上传文件的名字和文件存储系统的原有文件是否已经存在,
        此处返回False,让django认为传过来的文件都是新的, 让fdfs系统自己判断文件是否存在
        name: 用户选择上传文件的名称: logo.png
        """
        return False

    def url(self, name):
        """
        返回可访问到文件的完整的url地址:
        name: 数据库表中图片字段存放的内容，也就是'Remote file_id'的内容
        """
        return self.base_url + name


```

# 富文本编辑器ckeditor配置
CKEDITOR_CONFIGS = {
    'default': {
        'toolbar': 'full',  # 工具条功能
        'height': 300,  # 编辑器高度
        # 'width': 300,  # 编辑器宽
    },
}

### 10.9 商品model

```
from ckeditor.fields import RichTextField
from ckeditor_uploader.fields import RichTextUploadingField
```





```

class Spu(BaseModel):
    """
    商品SPU
    """
    name = models.CharField(max_length=60, verbose_name='名称')
    category1 = models.ForeignKey(GoodsCategory, on_delete=models.PROTECT, related_name='cat1_goods',verbose_name='一级类别')
    category2 = models.ForeignKey(GoodsCategory, on_delete=models.PROTECT, related_name='cat2_goods',verbose_name='二级类别')
    category3 = models.ForeignKey(GoodsCategory, on_delete=models.PROTECT, related_name='cat3_goods',verbose_name='三级类别')
    sold_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='销售数量')
    fav_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='收藏数量')
    comments_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='评价数量')
    goods_desc = RichTextUploadingField(default='', verbose_name='商品介绍')
    goods_pack = RichTextField(default='', verbose_name='包装信息')
    postsale_service = RichTextUploadingField(default='', verbose_name='售后服务')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '商品SPU'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return self.name


class Sku(BaseModel):
    """
    商品SKU
    """
    name = models.CharField(max_length=60, verbose_name='名称')
    sub_title = models.CharField(max_length=120, verbose_name='副标题')
    spu = models.ForeignKey(Spu, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='商品')
    sn = models.CharField("商品sn号", max_length=50, default="")
    category = models.ForeignKey(GoodsCategory, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name='从属三级类别')
    sale_price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, verbose_name='销售价')
    cost_price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, verbose_name='进价')
    stock_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='库存数量')
    sold_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='销售数量')
    comments_num = models.IntegerField(default=0, verbose_name='评论数量')
    is_online = models.BooleanField(default=True, verbose_name='是否上架销售')
    default_image_url = models.CharField(max_length=200, default='', null=True, blank=True, verbose_name='默认图片')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '商品SKU'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return '%s: %s' % (self.id, self.name)


# 商品轮播
class Banner(BaseModel):
    """
    首页banner
    """
    related_good = models.ForeignKey(Sku, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name='对应商品')
    image = models.ImageField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name='图片')
    sequence = models.IntegerField(verbose_name='排序')
    is_show = models.BooleanField(default=True, verbose_name='是否展示')


class AdvertisementCategory(BaseModel):
    """
    广告类别
    """
    name = models.CharField(max_length=30, verbose_name='名称')
    key = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='类别键名')
    sequence = models.IntegerField(verbose_name='排列顺序')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '广告类别'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return self.name


class Advertisement(BaseModel):
    """
    广告内容
    """
    related_good = models.ForeignKey(Sku, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name='对应商品')
    adv_category = models.ForeignKey(AdvertisementCategory, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name='广告类别')
    title = models.CharField(max_length=30, verbose_name='标题')
    sub_title = models.CharField(max_length=30, verbose_name='子标题')
    image = models.ImageField(null=True, blank=True, verbose_name='图片')
    sequence = models.IntegerField(verbose_name='排序')
    is_show = models.BooleanField(default=True, verbose_name='是否展示')
    tag = models.CharField(max_length=100, blank=True, null=True, verbose_name='标签')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '广告内容'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return self.category.name + ': ' + self.title



class SKUImage(BaseModel):
    """
    SKU图片
    """
    sku = models.ForeignKey(Sku, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='sku')
    image = models.ImageField(verbose_name='图片')

    class Meta:
        db_table = 'tb_sku_image'
        verbose_name = 'SKU图片'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return '%s %s' % (self.sku.name)
        
        

class SpuSpecification(BaseModel):
    """
    商品规格
    """
    spu = models.ForeignKey(Spu, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='商品Spu')
    name = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='规格名称')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '商品规格'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return '%s: %s' % (self.spu.name, self.name)


class SpecificationOption(BaseModel):
    """
    规格选项
    """
    spec = models.ForeignKey(SpuSpecification, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='商品规格')
    value = models.CharField(max_length=20, verbose_name='选项值')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '规格选项'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return '%s - %s' % (self.spec, self.value)

class SKUSpecification(BaseModel):
    """
    SKU具体规格
    """
    sku = models.ForeignKey(Sku, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='sku')
    option = models.ForeignKey(SpecificationOption, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name='规格值')

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = 'SKU规格'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name

    def __str__(self):
        return '%s: %s - %s' % (self.sku, self.option.spec.name, self.option.value)        
```

### 11.3 商品详情后端

修改goods/views.py 

添加GoodDetail

```
class GoodDetail(APIView):
    def get(self, request,sku_id):
        # -------获取当前sku的信息-------
        sku = Sku.objects.get(id=sku_id)
        sku.images = sku.skuimage_set.all()
        sku_image_list = []
        for image in sku.images:
            sku_image_list.append(image.image.url)
        sku_detail ={
            "title": sku.name,
            "sub_title": sku.sub_title,
            "sale_price": sku.sale_price,
            "category": sku.category.id,
            "sku_image_list": sku_image_list
        }
        
        # 获取对应的spu
        spu = sku.spu
        sku_info = {
            "comments_num": spu.comments_num,
            "goods_desc": spu.goods_desc,
            "goods_pack": spu.goods_pack,
            "postsale_service": spu.postsale_service
        }
        sku_detail.update(sku_info)
        



        # -------构建当前商品的规格键[1,5]-------
        # {1: '深空灰'}, {5: 'i5 8g 512g'}
        sku_specs = sku.skuspecification_set.order_by('option__spec_id')
        sku_key = []
        for spec in sku_specs:
            sku_key.append(spec.option.id)
            # sku_key.append({spec.option.id:spec.option.value})

        
        
        skus = spu.sku_set.all()

        '''
        # spec_sku_map = {
        #     (规格1参数id, 规格2参数id, 规格3参数id, ...): sku_id,
        #     (规格1参数id, 规格2参数id, 规格3参数id, ...): sku_id,
        #     ...
        # }
        "spec_sku_map": {
            "(1, 5)": 1,
            "(1, 6)": 2,
            "(1, 7)": 3,
            "(2, 7)": 4,
            "(2, 6)": 5,
            "(2, 5)": 6
        }
        '''
        spec_sku_map = {}
        for s in skus:
            # 获取所有的sku的规格参数
            s_specs = s.skuspecification_set.order_by('option__spec_id')
            # 规格参数的id列表
            key = []
            for spec in s_specs:
                key.append(spec.option.id)
            # 规格参数集合为字典键，对应的skuid为字典值


            # 此处需要判断如果规格只有1个的话需要特别处理
            key_str = str(tuple(key))
            if len(tuple(key)) == 1:
                key_str = key_str.replace(',','')
                spec_sku_map[key_str] = s.id
            else:
                spec_sku_map[key_str] = s.id

        specs = spu.spuspecification_set.order_by('id')

        # 获取所有的规格信息
        all_specs_info = []
        '''
         "all_specs_info": [
            {
                "name": "颜色",
                "options": [
                    {
                        "value": "深空灰",
                        "id": 1,
                        "checked": true
                    },
                    {
                        "value": "云杉绿",
                        "id": 2
                    }
                ]
            },
            {
                "name": "版本",
                "options": [
                    {
                        "value": "i5 8g 512g",
                        "id": 5
                    },
                    {
                        "value": "i7 8g 512g",
                        "id": 6,
                        "checked": true
                    },
                    {
                        "value": "i7 16g 512g",
                        "id": 7
                    }
                ]
            }
        ],
        '''
        # 若当前sku的规格信息不完整，则不再继续
        # if len(sku_key) < len(specs):
        #     return
        for index, spec in enumerate(specs):
            all_specs_dict = {}
            all_specs_dict['name'] = spec.name
            all_specs_info.append(all_specs_dict)
            options = spec.specificationoption_set.all()

            # 规格的value值
            option_list = []
            for option in options:
                # option_dict["value"] = option.value
                option_dict={}
                option_dict = {"value": option.value, "id": option.id}
                # 如果当前的规格值的id已经在当前sku的规格值里面，则代表选中状态
                if option.id in sku_key:
                    option_dict['checked'] = True
                option_list.append(option_dict)
                all_specs_dict['options'] = option_list
            # 复制当前sku的规格键
            # key = sku_key2[:]
            #
            # # 该规格的选项
            # options = spec.specificationoption_set.all()
            # for option in options:
            #     print("option", option)
            #     # 在规格参数sku字典中查找符合当前规格的sku
            #     key[index] = option.id
            #
            #     option.sku_id = spec_sku_map.get(str(tuple(key)))
            #     print("key=",key, " index=",index, "key[index]=",key[index],
            #           "option.id: ",option.id, "option.sku_id:",option.sku_id)
            #
            # spec.options = options

        final_result = {
            "sku_key": sku_key,
            "spec_sku_map": spec_sku_map,
            "all_specs_info": all_specs_info,
            "sku_detail": sku_detail
            # 'specs': specs
            # 'sku': sku
        }
        return Response(final_result)
```



修改goods/urls.py

```
   re_path(r'good/(?P<sku_id>\d+)/$', views.GoodDetail.as_view()),
```

```
<template>
    <div class="detail">
        <div class="wrapper">
            <div class="container clearfix">
                <div class="swiper clearfix" >
					<swiper :options="swiperOption">
                        <swiper-slide v-for="item in sku_detail.sku_image_list"
                        >

                        </swiper-slide>

                        <!-- Optional controls -->

                        <div class="swiper-button-prev" slot="button-prev"></div>
                        <div class="swiper-button-next" slot="button-next"></div>
                    </swiper>
                </div>

                    <h2 class="item-title">{{sku_detail.title}}</h2>
                    <p class="item-info">{{sku_detail.sub_title}}</p>
                    <div class="line"></div>
                    <div class="item-version clearfix" v-for="(item,index) in all_specs_info" :key="index">
                        <h2>{{item.name}}</h2>
                        <div @click="changeItem(option.id,index,i)"
                             class="item-detail fl" v-for="(option,i) in item.options"
                             :class="{'checked': option.checked}"

                        >
                            {{option.value}}
                        </div>

                    </div>

                    <div class="item-total">
                        <div class="item-info clearfix">
                            <div class="fl">{{sku_detail.title}}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="total-price">总计：{{sku_detail.sale_price}}元</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="btn-box">
                        <a href="javascript:;" class="cart fl">加入购物车</a>
                        <a href="javascript:;" class="fav fl">收藏</a>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="sales_info">
            <div class="hot_sales">
                <div class="sales-wrapper">
                    <h3>热销产品</h3>
                    <div>
                        <ul>
                            <li class="data-sku">
                                <div class="p-img">
                                    <img src="" alt="">
                                </div>
                                <div class="p-name">
                                    <em>Iphone</em>
                                </div>
                                <div class="p-price">
                                    <span class="price-title">售价: </span>
                                    <strong>￥20 </strong>
                                </div>


                            </li>
                        </ul>

                </div>

                    <el-tab-pane label="商品介绍" name="item-intro" v-html='sku_detail.goods_desc'></el-tab-pane>
                    <el-tab-pane label="规格与包装" v-html='sku_detail.goods_pack'></el-tab-pane>
                    <el-tab-pane label="售后保障" v-html='sku_detail.postsale_service'></el-tab-pane>
                    <el-tab-pane label="商品评价" v-html='sku_detail.comments_num'></el-tab-pane>
                </el-tabs>
            </div>

        </div>
    </div>
</template>
<script>
    import { getSku } from '@/api/Goods'
    export default{
        name:'detail',
        data(){
            return {
                id:this.$route.params.id,
                sku_detail: {},
                all_specs_info: [],
                sku_key: [],
                select_id:[],
                spec_sku_map: [],
                swiperOption:{
                    // autoplay:true,
                    pagination: {
                        el: '.swiper-pagination',
                        clickable :true,
                    },
                    navigation: {
                        nextEl: '.swiper-button-next',
                        prevEl: '.swiper-button-prev',
                    }
                },
                activeName: 'item-intro',
            }
        },
        computed: {
            swiper() {
                return this.$refs.mySwiper.$swiper
            }
        },
        methods:{
            _getSku() {
                getSku(this.id).then(res => {
                    this.sku_detail = res.sku_detail
                    this.all_specs_info = res.all_specs_info
                    this.sku_key = res.sku_key
                    this.select_id = res.sku_key
                    this.spec_sku_map = res.spec_sku_map
                    this.category_id = res.sku_detail.category
                })
            },
            // 改变规格选项
            changeItem(id, index,i ) {
                let spec = ""
                /*
                     id:当前商品id、
                     index:大规格的索引，具体点击的是颜色，还是版本
                     i：小规格的索引，点击的是颜色规格下的黑色，还是白色，
                     这里的index和i、用来控制点击项的高亮展示，同时需要id、push进对应索引的 select_id[]
                    */

                /*
                 this.select_id[index]
                 1.如果此时你点击的是第一项：颜色，那么 index == 0，循环this.all_specs_info[0].options
                 如果满足item.id == id 这个条件，就返回item这个数据，把该数据的id、赋值给this.select_id[0]
                 2.如果此时你点击的是第二项：颜色，那么 index == 1，循环this.all_specs_info[1].options
                 如果满足item.id == id 这个条件，就返回item这个数据，把该数据的id、赋值给this.select_id[1]
                */

                this.select_id[index] = this.all_specs_info[index].options.filter(item=>{
                    return item.id == id ;
                })[0].id;

                // 平凑"(1, 5)" 这样的Option_id转换为字符串
                this.select_id.forEach(item=>{
                    spec += item + ', '
                })
                spec = "(" + spec.substring(0,spec.length-2) + ")"
                let sku_id = this.spec_sku_map[spec]
                this.$router.push("/goods/" + sku_id)
                this.id = sku_id
                this._getSku()
            }
        },
        created() {
            this._getSku()
        },
        updated() {

        }
    }
</script>

### 11.5 后端热销商品

新建goods/serializers.py

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import Sku

class SkuSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    """商品序列化器类"""
    class Meta:
        model = Sku
        fields = ('id', 'name', 'sale_price', 'default_image_url')
```



修改goods/views.py

```
from goods.models import Sku
from .serializers import SkuSerializer
from rest_framework.generics import  ListAPIView


class HotGoodListView(ListAPIView):

    serializer_class = SkuSerializer

    def get_queryset(self):
        category_id = self.request.query_params.get('category')
        return Sku.objects.filter(category_id=category_id, is_online=True).order_by('-sold_num')[0:5]




```

修改goods/urls.py添加hotgood路由

```
   re_path(r'hotgoods/$', views.HotGoodListView.as_view()),

```



**drf缓存使用**

```
pip install drf-extensions
```

drf-extensions扩展对于缓存提供了三个扩展类：

```
ListCacheResponseMixin

用于缓存返回列表数据的视图，与ListModelMixin扩展类配合使用，

RetrieveCacheResponseMixin

用于缓存返回单一数据的视图，与RetrieveModelMixin扩展类配合使用，

CacheResponseMixin

为视图集同时补充List和Retrieve两种缓存，与ListModelMixin和RetrieveModelMixin一起配合使用。
```



修改settings/dev.py

将缓存数据保存在redis中，且设置有效期，

```
# DRF扩展
REST_FRAMEWORK_EXTENSIONS = {
    # 缓存时间
    'DEFAULT_CACHE_RESPONSE_TIMEOUT': 60 * 60,
    # 缓存存储
    'DEFAULT_USE_CACHE': 'default',
}
```





修改goods/views.py

添加ListCacheResponseMixin缓存

```
from rest_framework_extensions.cache.mixins import ListCacheResponseMixin


class HotGoodListView(ListCacheResponseMixin,ListAPIView):

    serializer_class = SkuSerializer

    def get_queryset(self):
        category_id = self.request.query_params.get('category')
        return Sku.objects.filter(category_id=category_id, is_online=True).order_by('-sale_price')[0:5]




```

import { getHotGoods } from '@/api/Goods'

                                    <em>{{hot_good.name}}</em>
                                </div>

                        this.sku_detail = res.sku_detail
                        this.all_specs_info = res.all_specs_info

### 12.3 楼层广告后台

修改goods/views.py

添加分类广告列表

```
class AdvertisementListView(APIView):
    def get(self, request):
        adv_categories = OrderedDict()
        advs = Advertisement.objects.filter(is_show=True).order_by('adv_category__sequence', 'sequence')
        for adv in advs:
            print("adv:",adv.image, adv.id)
            adv_category_id = adv.adv_category_id
            adv_name = adv.adv_category.name
            if adv_category_id not in adv_categories:
                adv_categories[adv_category_id] = { 'name': adv_name, 'adv_objs': [] }
            adv_categories[adv_category_id]['adv_objs'].append({
                'good_id': adv.related_good_id,
                'good_price': adv.related_good.sale_price,
                'title': adv.title,
                'sub_title': adv.sub_title,
                'image': adv.image.url,
                'tag': adv.tag
            })
        return Response(adv_categories)
```

```

# 13 商品列表页



### 13.1 商品列表后端



#新建goods/utils.py



```
from .models import GoodsCategory, Sku

# 获取商品种类是顶级还是第二级还是第三级
def getCategoryLevel(category_id):
    category_level = 0
    try:
        cat_obj = GoodsCategory.objects.get(id=category_id)
    except:
        raise Exception("错误的商品种类id")
    if cat_obj.parent is None:
        category_level = 1
    elif cat_obj.parent.parent is not None:
        category_level = 3
    else:
        category_level = 2
    return category_level



# 通过1级或者2级产品种类id获取循环下面的子种类获取对应商品
def getTopCategoryGoods(category_id):
    res = []
    category_level = getCategoryLevel(category_id)
    if category_level == 1:
        second_cat_level = GoodsCategory.objects.filter(parent=category_id)
        for second_obj in second_cat_level:
            third_cat_level = GoodsCategory.objects.filter(parent=second_obj)
            for third_obj in third_cat_level:
                res.append(third_obj.id)
    elif category_level == 2:
        third_cat_level = GoodsCategory.objects.filter(parent=category_id)
        for third_obj in third_cat_level:
            res.append(third_obj.id)
    else:
        res.append(category_id)
    return res
```



新建utils/pagination.py

```
# 自定义分页类
from rest_framework.pagination import PageNumberPagination


class StandardPagination(PageNumberPagination):
    # 指定默认页容量
    page_size = 4
    # 获取分页数据时页容量参数名称
    page_size_query_param = 'page_size'
    # 每页上限
    max_page_size = 20
```





修改goods/views.py

```
from xiaofu.utils.pagination import StandardPagination
from rest_framework.filters import OrderingFilter
from .utils import getCategoryLevel, getThirdCategories

class SKUListView(ListAPIView):
    # 指定当前视图所使用的查询集
    # queryset = SKU.objects.filter(category_id=category_id, is_launched=True)
    serializer_class = SkuSerializer
    pagination_class = StandardPagination

    # 排序
    filter_backends = [OrderingFilter]
    # 指定排序字段
    ordering_fields = ('create_time', 'sale_price', 'sold_num')

    def get_queryset(self):
        """返回视图使用的查询集"""
        category_id = self.request.query_params.get('category')
        
        res = getThirdCategories(category_id)
        return Sku.objects.filter(category_id__in=res, is_online=True)
```

修改goods/urls.py

```
   re_path(r'list/$', views.SKUListView.as_view()),

```

### 13.2 商品列表前端

基础页面

新建Goods/List.vue

修改Goods/List.vue

引入el-pagination分页 获取后端数据



```
<template>
    <div>
        <div class="product-box">
            <div class="container">
                <div class="wrapper">
                    <div class="list-box">
                        <div class="list">
                            <div class="item" v-for="good in goods">
                               
                                <div class="item-img"><img :src="good.default_image_url" alt=""></div>
                                <div class="item-info">
                                    <p>{{good.name}}</p>
                                    <p class="price">¥{{good.sale_price}}元</p>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="page">
                    <el-pagination
                            :page-size="page_size"
                            background
                            layout="pager"
                            :total=count
                            :current-page="page"
                            @current-change = "changePage"

                    >
                    </el-pagination>
                </div>

            </div>

        </div>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    import { getGoodsList } from '@/api/Goods'

    export default {
        name: "List",
        data() {
            return {
 				goods: [],
                count: 0,
                page: 1, // 当前页数
                page_size: 4, // 每页数量
                ordering: '-create_time', // 排序
                
            }
        },
		computed: {
            category: {
                get: function () {
                    return this.$route.query.category
                },
                set: function (newValue) {

                }

            }
        },

        methods: {
            _getGoodsList: function(){
                let params = {
                    category: this.category,
                    page: this.page,
                    page_size: this.page_size,
                    ordering: this.ordering
                }
                getGoodsList(params).then(res => {
                    this.count = res.count;
                    this.goods = res.results
                })
            },
            changePage(page_num) {
                this.page = page_num
                this._getGoodsList()
            }
        },
        created() {
            this._getGoodsList()
        }
    }
</script>

<style scoped lang="stylus">

    
    .product-box {
        

        .page {

            width 100%
            text-align center
            background-color: #fff;
        }
    }

</style>

```
data {
    ordering_class: 'create_time_class',
}

methods: {		
		
		on_sort(ordering){
                console.log(ordering)
                if (ordering != this.ordering) {
                    this.page = 1;
                    this.ordering = ordering;
                    this.ordering_class = ordering + "_class"
                    this._getGoodsList();
                } else {
                    this.page = 1;
                    this.ordering = "-"+ordering;
                    this._getGoodsList();
                }
            },
        }

### 13.4 面包屑后端

修改goods/utils.py

获取面包屑

```
def getBreadCrumb(category_id):
    try:
        cat_obj = GoodsCategory.objects.get(id=category_id)
    except:
        raise Exception("错误的商品种类id")
    if cat_obj.parent is None:
        return { "cat_top_obj": {"cat_obj_name": cat_obj.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.id }}
    elif cat_obj.parent.parent is not None:
        return {"cat_third_obj": { "cat_obj_name": cat_obj.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.id },
                "cat_second_obj": { "cat_obj_name": cat_obj.parent.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.parent.id},
                "cat_top_obj": {"cat_obj_name": cat_obj.parent.parent.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.parent.parent.id }
                }
    else:
        return { "cat_second_obj": { "cat_obj_name": cat_obj.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.id},
                 "cat_top_obj": { "cat_obj_name": cat_obj.parent.name, "cat_obj_id": cat_obj.parent.id }
              }
```



修改good/views.py

添加BreadCrumb

```
from .utils import getBreadCrumb


class BreadCrumb(APIView):
    def get(self, request):
        category_id = request.query_params.get('category')
        category_stru = getBreadCrumb(category_id)
        return Response(category_stru)
```



修改goods/urls.py

添加面包屑导航

```

```

需要使用watch $route，当路由发生变化时候重新加载页面

computed里面的category需要使用 setter 当category发生变化时候重新给category赋值

```
import { getBreadCrumb } from '@/api/Goods'


methods: {
    _getBreadCrumb() {
                let params = {
                    category: this.category,
                }
                getBreadCrumb(params).then(res => {
                    console.log("resssssss", res)
                    this.three_category = res
                    console.log("three_category",this.three_category)
                })


            },
}

 created() {
           
            this._getBreadCrumb()
        }
        
        
        watch: {
            $route (to, from) {
                this.category = to.query.category
                this.ordering = 'create_time'
                this.page = 1

                this.changePage(1)
                this._getBreadCrumb()
            }
        },
        
        
        computed: {
            category: {
                get: function () {
                    return this.$route.query.category
                },
                set: function (newValue) {

                }

            }
        },
```

# 14 购物车

### 14.1 购物车后端添加商品

用户必须登录使用redis来保存购物车数据

```
# 某用户购物车里所有数据(包含勾选和非勾选的商品)
# hash类型保存
cart_用户ID: {sku_id1: count, sku_id2: count, sku_id3: count  ... }

# 某用户购物车的勾选记录 使用set保存
cart_selected_用户ID：{sku_id1, skuid_2  ...}
```



新建cart app

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py startapp cart
```

```
CACHES = {
"cart": {
        "BACKEND": "django_redis.cache.RedisCache",
        "LOCATION": "redis://192.168.70.101:6379/3",
        "OPTIONS": {
            "CLIENT_CLASS": "django_redis.client.DefaultClient",
        }
    },
}
```







新建cart/serializers.py

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from goods.models import Sku

class CartSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    sku_id = serializers.IntegerField(label='商品SKUID')
    count = serializers.IntegerField(label='商品数量', min_value=1)
    selected = serializers.BooleanField(label='商品勾选状态', default=True)

    def validate(self, attrs):
        # 获取ski_id判断商品是否存在
        sku_id = attrs['sku_id']

        try:
            sku = Sku.objects.get(id=sku_id)
        except Sku.DoesNotExist:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('商品不存在')

        # 判断要买的商品数量是否大于库存
        count = attrs['count']
        if count > sku.stock_num:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('商品库存不足')

        return attrs
```









新建cart/views.py

添加购物车逻辑

```
from django_redis import get_redis_connection
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework import status
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated

from .serializers import CartSerializer

class CartView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def post(self, request):
        """
        添加购物车记录
        """
        # 1. 获取参数(sku_id, count, selected)并进行参数校验
        serializer = CartSerializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

        sku_id = serializer.validated_data['sku_id']
        count = serializer.validated_data['count']
        selected = serializer.validated_data['selected']

        # 获取登录用户
        user = request.user

        # 保存用户的购物车记录
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')
        pipeline = redis_conn.pipeline()
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id

        # 保存购物车中商品sku_id以及对应数量count, count可以是负数
        pipeline.hincrby(cart_key, sku_id, count)

        # 保存购物车中商品的选中状态
        cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id
        if selected:
            pipeline.sadd(cart_selected_key, sku_id)

        pipeline.execute()
        
        num = redis_conn.scard(cart_selected_key)
        serializer_data = serializer.data

        serializer_data.update({"total": num})

        # 返回应答，保存购物车记录成功
        return Response(serializer_data, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
```



修改最外层urls.py

添加cart

```
    path('', include('cart.urls')),

```



新建cart/urls.py

```
from django.urls import re_path
from cart import views


urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'cart/$', views.CartView.as_view()),
]
```

#查看redis购物车情况

```
127.0.0.1:6379[3]> keys *
1) "cart_selected_2"
2) "cart_2"
127.0.0.1:6379[3]> hgetall cart_2
1) "1"
2) "6"
3) "2"
4) "12"
127.0.0.1:6379[3]> smembers cart_selected_2
1) "1"
2) "2"
127.0.0.1:6379[3]> scard cart_selected_2
(integer) 2
```

    return axios.post('/cart/', params, {

    })
}

新建store/cart.js

使用cartCount保存购物车总数

```
const cart = {
    state: {
        cartCount: 0
    },
    mutations: {
        GET_CART_COUNT(state, count) {
            state.cartCount = count;
        }
    },
    actions: {  },
    getters: {  }
}

export default cart
```

```
    import { addCart } from '@/api/Cart'
    import {mapMutations, mapState} from 'vuex'

		computed: {
            ...mapState({
                'isLogin': state=> state.user.isLogin,
            })
        },


			_addCart() {
                if (!this.isLogin) {
                    let current_path = this.$route.path
                    this.$router.push({ name: 'login', query: {'next': current_path} })
                  
                } else {
                    let params = {"sku_id": this.id, "count": 1, "selected": true}
                    addCart(params).then(res => {
                        this.GET_CART_COUNT(res.total)
                        this.$message.success('加入购物车成功');
                    })
                }
            },
            ...mapMutations(['GET_CART_COUNT'])
```

### 14.3 购物车后端统计商品总数

修改cart/views.py

添加CartCountView，根据用户是否登录来获取购物车总数

```
class CartCountView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def get(self, request):
        # 获取登录用户
       
        user = request.user
        
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
        cart_total_quantity = redis_conn.hlen(cart_key)

        return Response({"cart_count": cart_total_quantity})
```

修改cart/urls.py

添加路由

```
re_path(r'cart/count/$', views.CartCountView.as_view())
```

### 14.5 购物车列表后端

修改cart/serializers.py

添加CartListSerializer

```
class CartListSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    count = serializers.IntegerField(label='商品数量')
    selected = serializers.BooleanField(label='是否勾选')
    total_price = serializers.FloatField(label='商品总价')

    class Meta:
        model = Sku
        fields = ('id', 'name', 'sale_price', 'default_image_url', 'count', 'selected', 'stock_num', 'total_price')

```



修改cart/views.py

下的CartView

```
    	def get(self, request):      
    		user = request.user
    	
            # 2.1 如果用户已登录，从redis中获取用户的购物车记录
            # 获取redis链接
            redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')

            # 从redis中获取用户购物车中添加的商品sku_id和对应数量count hash
            cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
            
             # 从redis中获取用户购物车勾选商品sku_id set
            cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id
            
            # 获取购物车中商品的总数量
            cart_total_quantity = redis_conn.hlen(cart_key)
            
            # 获取购物车中勾选商品的数量
            cart_selected_total_quantity = redis_conn.scard(cart_selected_key)
            
            # 全部勾选状态
            all_selected = False
            if cart_selected_total_quantity == cart_total_quantity:
                all_selected = True
            
            
            
            sku_ids = redis_conn.hkeys(cart_key)
            sku_ids = list(map(int,sku_ids))
            # 
            skus = Sku.objects.filter(id__in=sku_ids)
            
            cart_selected_sku_ids = redis_conn.smembers(cart_selected_key)

        	cart_total_price = 0

            for sku in skus:
                # 给sku对象增加属性count和selected
                # 分别保存用户购物车中添加的该商品的数量和勾选状态
                sku.count = int(redis_conn.hget(cart_key, sku.id))
                sku.selected = str(sku.id).encode() in cart_selected_sku_ids
                sku.total_price = sku.count * sku.sale_price
                if sku.selected:
                    cart_total_price += sku.total_price


            serializer = CartListSerializer(skus, many=True)
            result = {"cart_list": serializer.data,
                      "cart_total_price": cart_total_price,
                      "cart_total_quantity": cart_total_quantity,
                      "all_selected": all_selected,
                      "cart_selected_total_quantity": cart_selected_total_quantity
                      }
            return Response(result)
```

### 14.7 购物车更新后端 

修改cart/views.py

下的CartView

```
    def put(self,request):
        serializer = CartSerializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

        # 获取参数
        sku_id = serializer.validated_data['sku_id']
        count = serializer.validated_data['count']
        selected = serializer.validated_data['selected']

    
        # 获取redis链接
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')
        pl = redis_conn.pipeline()

        # 修改redis用户购物车中商品id和数量count hash
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
        # hset(key, field, value):
        pl.hset(cart_key, sku_id, count)

        # 修改redis用户购物车中商品的勾选状态 set
        cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id

        if selected:
        # 勾选
        pl.sadd(cart_selected_key, sku_id)
        else:
        # 不勾选
        pl.srem(cart_selected_key, sku_id)
        pl.execute()
        return Response("更新成功")
```





![](水印pics\购物车更新.jpg)







### 14.8 购物车更新前端

更新分为点击+-按钮，点击是否选择某商品，以及选择商品数量

修改api/Cart.js

```
const updateCart = (params) => {
    return axios.put('/cart/', params, {
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}

export { updateCart }
```



```
<span class="checkbox" :class="{'checked':item.selected}" @click="updateMyCart(item)"></span>


  <div class="item-num">
                        <div class="num-box">
                            <a href="javascript:;" @click="updateMyCart(item,'-')">-</a>
<!--                            <span>{{item.count}}</span>-->
                            <input v-model="item.count" class="count" @focus="origin_input=item.count" @blur="check_input(item)">

                            <a href="javascript:;" @click="updateMyCart(item,'+')">+</a>
                        </div>
                    </div>
```



```
data() {
            return {
            	origin_input: 0 // 用于记录手动输入前的值
            }
        }    
	
methods: {	
	check_input(item) {
                let count = item.count,
                    selected = item.selected;
                if (isNaN(count) || count <= 0) {
                    item.count = this.origin_input;
                } else if (count > item.stock_num) {
                    item.count = this.origin_input;
                    this.$message.warning('购买数量不能超过库存数量');
                } else {
                    this._updateCart({
                        sku_id: item.id,
                        count: count,
                        selected: selected
                    })
                }

            },

            updateMyCart(item,type){
                let count = item.count,
                    selected = item.selected;
                if(type == '-'){
                    if(count == 1){
                        this.$message.warning('商品至少保留一件');
                        return;
                    }
                    --count;
                }else if(type == '+'){
                    if(count > item.stock_num){
                        this.$message.warning('购买数量不能超过库存数量');
                        return;
                    }
                    ++count;
                }else{
                    selected = !item.selected;
                }
                this._updateCart({
                    sku_id: item.id,
                    count: count,
                    selected: selected
                })
            },

            _updateCart(params) {
                updateCart(params).then(res => {
                    this._getCartList()
                })
            },
  }          
```





### 14.9 购物车全选后端

修改cart/serializers.py

添加CartToggleSerializer

```
class CartToggleSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    selected = serializers.BooleanField(label='是否全选')
```





修改cart/views.py

新建CartToggleView

```
class CartToggleView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def put(self, request):
        # 1. 接收参数selected并进行校验(必传)
        serializer = CartToggleSerializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

		user = request.user

        # 获取参数
        selected = serializer.validated_data['selected']
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')

        # 获取购物车中所有的商品id
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
        sku_ids = redis_conn.hkeys(cart_key)

        # 设置redis用户购物车记录勾选状态 set
        cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id
        if selected:
            # 全选
            # sadd(key, *members)
            redis_conn.sadd(cart_selected_key, *sku_ids)
            return Response({'detail': '购物车全选成功'})
        else:
            # 全不选
            # srem(key, *members)
            redis_conn.srem(cart_selected_key, *sku_ids)
            return Response({'detail': '取消购物车全选成功'})

```



修改cart/urls.py

```
re_path(r'cart/toggle/$', views.CartToggleView.as_view())
```
