toggle() {
                let all_selected_flag = this.cartAllSelected ? false: true

                    this._getCartList()
                })
            },
```





### 14.11 购物车删除后端

修改cart/serializers.py 

添加CartDelSerializer

```
class CartDelSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    """购物车删除序列化器类"""
    sku_id = serializers.IntegerField(label='商品Sku编号')

    def validate_sku_id(self, value):
        """sku_id对应的商品是否存在"""
        try:
            sku = Sku.objects.get(id=value)
        except Sku.DoesNotExist:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('商品不存在')

        return value
```





修改cart/views.py下的CartView

添加购物车删除 delete逻辑

```
    def delete(self, request):
        # 1. 获取商品sku_id并进行校验(必传，sku_id对应的商品是否存在)
        serializer = CartDelSerializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

		user = request.user

        sku_id = serializer.validated_data['sku_id']


        # 获取redis链接
        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')
        pl = redis_conn.pipeline()

        # 删除购物车中的商品
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
        pl.hdel(cart_key, sku_id)

        # 勾选商品中删除，若无则忽略
        cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id
        pl.srem(cart_selected_key, sku_id)

        pl.execute()

        return Response({'detail': '删除成功'}, status=status.HTTP_204_NO_CONTENT)
```

新建orders/serializers.py

```
from rest_framework import serializers
from cart.serializers import CartListSerializer

class OrderConfirmSerializer(serializers.Serializer):
    freight = serializers.DecimalField(label='运费', max_digits=8, decimal_places=2)
    order_items_total_price = serializers.DecimalField(label='商品总价', max_digits=20, decimal_places=2)
    order_total_price = serializers.DecimalField(label='应付金额', max_digits=20, decimal_places=2)
    order_items_total_quantity = serializers.IntegerField(label='商品总数', min_value=1)
    skus = CartListSerializer(many=True)

    def validate(self, attrs):
        order_total_price = attrs['order_total_price']
        order_items_total_quantity = attrs['order_items_total_quantity']
        if order_total_price <= 0:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('总价小于0')
        if order_items_total_quantity < 0:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('商品数量至少一件')
```



新建order/views.py

```
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated
from rest_framework.response import Response
from django_redis import get_redis_connection
from decimal import Decimal

from goods.models import Sku

from .serializers import OrderConfirmSerializer

# Create your views here.

class OrderConfirmView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

        def get(self, request):
        user = request.user

        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')
        cart_select_key = 'cart_selected_%s' %user.id
        cart_key = 'cart_%s' %user.id
        sku_ids = redis_conn.smembers(cart_select_key)
        sku_ids = list(map(int, sku_ids))

        skus = Sku.objects.filter(id__in=sku_ids)
        order_items_total_price = 0

        for sku in skus:
            sku.count = int(redis_conn.hget(cart_key, sku.id))
            sku.selected = True
            sku.total_price = sku.count * sku.sale_price
            order_items_total_price += sku.total_price

        order_items_total_quantity = redis_conn.scard(cart_select_key)
        freight = Decimal(10)
        order_total_price = order_items_total_price + freight

        resp = {
            'freight': freight,
            'skus': skus,
            'order_items_total_quantity': order_items_total_quantity,
            'order_items_total_price': order_items_total_price,
            'order_total_price': order_total_price
        }

        serializer = OrderConfirmSerializer(resp)
        return Response(serializer.data)
```



新建order/urls.py

from django.urls import re_path
from rest_framework import routers

from order import views




urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'order/confirm/$', views.OrderConfirmView.as_view()),
]

import axios from '@/utils/request'
import { getToken } from "@/utils/token";


const orderConfirm = () => {

    return axios.get('/order/confirm/', '', {
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}

export { orderConfirm }
```



Order/OrderConfirm.vue

```
    import { orderConfirm } from '@/api/Order'


data() {
            return {
                orderList: [],
                orderItemsTotalPrice: 0,
                orderItemsTotalQunatity: 0,
                orderTotalPrice: 0,
                freight: 0
            }
        },
        methods: {
            _orderConfirm() {
                orderConfirm().then(res => {
                    this.freight = res.freight
                    this.orderList = res.skus
                    this.orderItemsTotalPrice = res.order_items_total_price
                    this.orderItemsTotalQunatity = res.order_items_total_quantity
                    this.orderTotalPrice = res.order_total_price
                })
            }
        },
        created() {
            this._orderConfirm()
        }
```

##### 15.2.3地址信息

```
import { getAddressList } from '@/api/Account'

data() {
            return {
               
                checkedAddressIndex: 0,
                checkedAddressId: 0,
                default_address_id: 0,
                addressList: []
            }
        },


			_getAddressList() {
                getAddressList().then(res => {
                    this.addressList = res.addresses
                    this.default_address_id = res.default_address_id
                    this.checkedAddressId = this.default_address_id

                    this.addressList.forEach((item, index)=> {
                        if(item.id === this.default_address_id) {
                            this.checkedAddressIndex = index
                        }
                    })
                })
            }
            
            
        created() {
            this._getAddressList()
        }
```

### 15.3 订单信息Model

order/Models.py

```
from django.db import models
from xiaofu.utils.models import BaseModel
from users.models import User, Address
from goods.models import Sku


# Create your models here.


class OrderInfo(BaseModel):
    """
    订单信息
    """
    PAY_METHODS_ENUM = {
        "UNSELECTED": 0,
        "WECHAT": 1,
        "ALIPAY": 2
    }

    PAY_METHOD_CHOICES = (
        (0, "未选择"),
        (1, "微信"),
        (2, "支付宝"),
    )

    ORDER_STATUS_ENUM = {
        "UNPAID": 1,
        "UNSEND": 2,
        "UNRECEIVED": 3,
        "UNCOMMENT": 4,
        "FINISHED": 5
    }

    ORDER_STATUS_CHOICES = (
        (1, "待支付"),
        (2, "待发货"),
        (3, "待收货"),
        (4, "待评价"),
        (5, "已完成"),
        (6, "已取消"),
    )

    order_id = models.CharField(max_length=60, primary_key=True, verbose_name="订单号")
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name="订单用户")
    address = models.ForeignKey(Address, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name="收获地址")
    total_quantity = models.IntegerField(default=1, verbose_name="商品总数")
    total_price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, verbose_name="商品总金额")
    freight = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, verbose_name="运费")
    pay_method = models.SmallIntegerField(choices=PAY_METHOD_CHOICES, default=0, verbose_name="支付方式")
    status = models.SmallIntegerField(choices=ORDER_STATUS_CHOICES, default=1, verbose_name="订单状态")

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '订单信息'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name


class OrderGoods(BaseModel):
    order = models.ForeignKey(OrderInfo, related_name='skus', on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name="所属订单")
    sku = models.ForeignKey(Sku, on_delete=models.PROTECT, verbose_name="订单商品")
    quantity = models.IntegerField(default=1, verbose_name="商品数量")
    sale_price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2, verbose_name="销售价格")

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '订单商品'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name




```



```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py makemigrations
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py migrate
```









### 15.4 订单保存后端



修改order/serializers.py

添加保存订单OrderSaveSerializer

```
from django.db import transaction
from django_redis import get_redis_connection

from datetime import datetime
from decimal import Decimal

from .models import OrderInfo, OrderGoods
from goods.models import Sku

class OrderSaveSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = OrderInfo
        fields = ('order_id', 'address')
        read_only_fields = ('order_id',)
        write_only_fields = ('address',)

    def create(self, validated_data):

        address = validated_data['address']
        user = self.context['request'].user

        # 订单id: '年月日时分秒'+用户id
        order_id = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d%H%M%S') + ('%08d' % user.id)

        freight = Decimal(10)

        redis_conn = get_redis_connection('cart')

        cart_key = 'cart_%s' % user.id
        sku_ids = redis_conn.hkeys(cart_key)
        sku_ids = list(map(int, sku_ids))

        cart_selected_key = 'cart_selected_%s' % user.id
        sku_ids = redis_conn.smembers(cart_selected_key)
        total_quantity = redis_conn.scard(cart_selected_key)



        with transaction.atomic():
            # 在with语句块中代码，凡是涉及到数据库操作的代码，都会放到同一个事务中

            # 设置一个事务保存点
            sid = transaction.savepoint()
            try:
                order = OrderInfo.objects.create(
                    order_id=order_id,
                    user=user,
                    address=address,
                    total_quantity=total_quantity,
                    total_price=Decimal(0.00),
                    freight=freight
                )

                sku_list = Sku.objects.filter(id__in=sku_ids)

                for sku in sku_list:
                    # 如果购物车的商品数量小于库存，则回滚
                    item_quantity = int(redis_conn.hget(cart_key, sku.id))
                    print("item_quantity", item_quantity)
                    if sku.stock_num < item_quantity:
                        transaction.savepoint_rollback(sid)
                        raise serializers.ValidationError('商品库存不足')

                    # 库存充足则把库存减去购物车商品数量，随后销售数量加上购物车商品数量
                    sku.stock_num -= item_quantity
                    sku.sold_num += item_quantity
                    sku.save()

                    # 计算总金额和总数量
                    
                    order.total_price += sku.sale_price * item_quantity

                    # 创建订单商品对象
                    OrderGoods.objects.create(
                        order = order,
                        sku = sku,
                        quantity = item_quantity,
                        sale_price = sku.sale_price
                    )
                order.save()

            except serializers.ValidationError as e:
                raise e
            except Exception as e:
                transaction.savepoint_rollback(sid)
                raise e


            transaction.savepoint_commit(sid)


            pl = redis_conn.pipeline()
            pl.hdel(cart_key, *sku_ids)
            pl.srem(cart_selected_key, *sku_ids)
            pl.execute()

            return order
```





修改order/views.py

```
from rest_framework.generics import CreateAPIView

class OrderSaveView(CreateAPIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]
    serializer_class = OrderSaveSerializer
```



修改order/urls.py

```
   re_path(r'order/save/$', views.OrderSaveView.as_view()),
```

### 15.6 并发问题

修改order/serializers.py 下的OrderSaveSerializer下的create方法

                    # 模拟并发查库存
                    import time
                    time.sleep(5)
```
                for sku in sku_list:
                    # 如果购物车的商品数量小于库存，则回滚
                    item_quantity = cart[sku.id]
                    if sku.stock_num < item_quantity:
                        transaction.savepoint_rollback(sid)
                        raise serializers.ValidationError('商品库存不足')

                    import time
                    time.sleep(5)

                    # 库存充足则把库存减去购物车商品数量，随后销售数量加上购物车商品数量
                    sku.stock_num -= item_quantity
                    sku.sold_num += item_quantity
                    sku.save()
```



修改某个sku库存为1

![](水印pics\并发库存.png)

使用2个不同的用户同时选择上面的sku商品并且同时点击结算，可以看到订单都支付成功了



![](水印pics\订单1.jpg)



![](水印pics\订单2.jpg)

再次查询库存发现为0了

![](水印pics\并发2.jpg)





解决方案

- **悲观锁**

  当查询某条记录时，即让数据库为该记录加锁，锁住记录后别人无法操作，使用类似如下语法

  ```python
  select stock from sku where id=1 for update;
  
  Sku.objects.select_for_update().get(id=1)
  ```

  悲观锁容易出现死锁，所以采用不多。

- **乐观锁**

  乐观锁并不是真实存在的锁，而是在更新的时候判断此时的库存是否是之前查询出的库存，如果相同，表示没人修改，可以更新库存，否则表示别人抢过资源，不再执行库存更新。类似如下操作

  ```python
  update tb_sku set stock_num=2 where id=1 and stock_num=6;
  
  SKU.objects.filter(id=1, stock_num=6).update(stock_num=2)
  ```

- **任务队列**

  将下单的逻辑放到任务队列中（如celery），将并行转为串行，所有人排队下单。比如开启只有一个进程的Celery，一个订单一个订单的处理。



并发代码修改order/serlizers.py



```
获取sku_id_list = cart.keys(),循环获取sku = Sku.objects.get(id=sku_id)
# 注释一下代码
# sku.stock_num -= item_quantity
                        # sku.sold_num += item_quantity
                        # sku.save()
                        
                        
                        # 编写新代码
                        new_stock_num = origin_stock_num - item_quantity
                        new_sold_num = origin_sold_num + item_quantity

                        res = Sku.objects.filter(id=sku.id, stock_num=origin_stock_num) \
                                        .update(stock_num = new_stock_num, sold_num = new_sold_num)

                        if res == 0:
                            continue
```



```
                for sku in sku_list:
                    while True:
                        item_quantity = int(redis_conn.hget(cart_key, sku.id))
                        if sku.stock_num < item_quantity:
                            transaction.savepoint_rollback(sid)
                            raise serializers.ValidationError('商品库存不足')

                        origin_stock_num = sku.stock_num
                        origin_sold_num = sku.sold_num

                        print("origin_stock_num", origin_stock_num)

                        new_stock_num = origin_stock_num - item_quantity
                        new_sold_num = origin_sold_num + item_quantity

                        import time
                        time.sleep(8)

                        # sku.stock_num -= item_quantity
                        # sku.sold_num += item_quantity
                        # sku.save()


                        res = Sku.objects.filter(id=sku.id, stock_num=origin_stock_num) \
                            .update(stock_num=new_stock_num, sold_num=new_sold_num)

                        sku.stock_num = new_stock_num
                        if res==0:
                            continue

                        order.total_price += sku.sale_price * item_quantity

                        OrderGoods.objects.create(order=order, sku=sku, quantity=item_quantity,
                                                  sale_price=sku.sale_price)
                        break
                order.save()
```





### 15.7 订单支付后端

修改order/serializers.py

```
from users.serializers import AddressSerializer
from goods.serializers import SkuSerializer

class OrderPaySerialzier(serializers.Serializer):
    order_total_price = serializers.DecimalField(label='应付金额', max_digits=20, decimal_places=2)
    skus = SkuSerializer(many=True)
    address = AddressSerializer(many=False)
```



修改order/views.py

```
class OrderPay(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def get(self, request):
        user = request.user
        order_id = request.query_params.get('order_id')
        orderInfo_obj = OrderInfo.objects.get(order_id=order_id)
        address = orderInfo_obj.address

        order_total_price = orderInfo_obj.freight + orderInfo_obj.total_price
        # orderGoodsObj = orderInfo_obj.skus.all()
        orderGoods_obj = OrderGoods.objects.filter(order_id=order_id)
        sku_list = []
        for good in orderGoods_obj:
            sku_list.append(good.sku.id)
        skus = Sku.objects.filter(id__in=sku_list)

        resp = {
            "order_total_price": order_total_price,
            "skus": skus,
            "address": address
        }

        serializer = OrderPaySerialzier(resp)
        return Response(serializer.data)
```



修改Order/urls.py

```
urlpatterns = [
  
   re_path(r'order/pay/$', views.OrderPay.as_view()),
]
```

修改Order.js

添加orderPayInfo接口

```
const orderPayInfo = (params) => {
    return axios.get('/order/pay/', params, {
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}
```



修改Order/OrderPay.vue

渲染页面

```
import { orderPayInfo } from '@/api/Order'

    export default{
        name:'order-pay',
        data(){
            return {
                orderId:this.$route.query.order_id,
                address: {},
                order_total_price: 0,
                sku_list: []

            }
        },
        components:{
            OrderHeader
        },
        methods:{
            _orderPayInfo() {
                orderPayInfo({'order_id': this.orderId}).then(res => {
                    this.address = res.address
                    this.order_total_price = res.order_total_price
                    this.sku_list = res.skus
                })
            }
        },
        created() {
            this._orderPayInfo()
        }
    }
```

修改payment/models.py

```
from django.db import models

from xiaofu.utils.models import BaseModel
from order.models import OrderInfo


# Create your models here.


class Payment(BaseModel):
    order = models.ForeignKey(OrderInfo, on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='订单')
    trade_id = models.CharField(max_length=60, unique=True, null=True, blank=True, verbose_name="支付编号")

    class Meta:
        verbose_name = '支付信息'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name
```



```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py makemigrations
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py migrate
```

修改payment/views.py

添加AliPayView

```
import os

from django.conf import settings
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework import status
from rest_framework.response import Response
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from rest_framework.permissions import IsAuthenticated

from alipay import AliPay

from order.models import OrderInfo
from payment.models import Payment
# Create your views here.

class AliPayView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def get(self, request, order_id):
        """
        获取支付宝支付网址和参数:
        1. 根据订单id校验订单是否有效
        2. 组织支付宝支付网址和参数
        3. 返回支付支付网址
        """
        user = request.user
        print(user, order_id, OrderInfo.PAY_METHODS_ENUM['ALIPAY'], )
        # 1. 根据订单id校验订单是否有效
        try:
            order = OrderInfo.objects.get(
                order_id=order_id,
                user=user,
                status=OrderInfo.ORDER_STATUS_ENUM['UNPAID'], # 待支付
            )
        except OrderInfo.DoesNotExist:
            return Response({'message': '无效的订单信息'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        # 2. 组织支付宝支付网址和参数
        # 初始化
        # print(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
        # print(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)),"keys/app_private_key.pem"))

        app_private_key_string = open(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)),"keys/app_private_key.pem")).read()
        print("app_private_key_string:", app_private_key_string)
        alipay_public_key_string = open(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)),
                                                "keys/alipay_public_key.pem")).read()
        print("alipay_public_key_string:",alipay_public_key_string)
        alipay_client = AliPay(
            appid=settings.ALIPAY_APPID, # 应用APPID
            # appid='2016092500594764', # 应用APPID
            app_notify_url=None,  # 默认回调url
            app_private_key_string=app_private_key_string,
            alipay_public_key_string=alipay_public_key_string,  # 支付宝的公钥，验证支付宝回传消息使用，不是你自己的公钥,
            sign_type="RSA2",  # RSA 或者 RSA2
            debug=settings.ALIPAY_DEBUG  # 默认False
        )

        # 组织支付参数
        # 电脑网站支付，需要跳转到https://openapi.alipay.com/gateway.do? + order_string
        total_amount = order.total_price # Decimal
        order_string = alipay_client.api_alipay_trade_page_pay(
            out_trade_no=order_id, # 商户订单号
            total_amount=str(total_amount), # 订单总金额
            subject='小福商城%s' % order_id, # 订单标题
            return_url="http://127.0.0.1:8080/alipays_success.html",
            notify_url=None  # 可选, 不填则使用默认notify url
        )

        # 3. 返回支付支付网址
        pay_url = settings.ALIPAY_URL + '?' + order_string
        return Response({'alipay_url': pay_url})

```



修改settings/dev.py

添加支付宝相关配置

```
# 支付宝
ALIPAY_APPID = "2016092500594764" # 开发应用APPID
ALIPAY_URL = "https://openapi.alipaydev.com/gateway.do" # 支付宝网关地址
ALIPAY_DEBUG = True # 是否使用沙箱环境

const orderAlipay = (orderId) => {
    return axios.get('/order/alipay/' + orderId + '/', '', {
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}


export { orderAlipay }
```



修改Order/OrderPay.vue

通过payTypeSelect来高亮显示

payConfirm判断是支付宝支付还是微信支付进行跳转

```
    import { orderAlipay } from '@/api/Order'

	data(){
            return {
              
                payType:'',//支付类型

            }
        },
	
	methods:{
           
            payTypeSelect(payType) {
                this.payType = payType
            },
            payConfirm() {
                if (this.payType == 1) {
                    orderAlipay(this.orderId).then(res => {
                        window.open(res.alipay_url)
                    })
                    // window.open('/#/order/alipay?orderId=' + this.orderId, '_blank');
                } else {
                    // this.payType = 2
                }
            }
        },
```





通过payType动态绑定class

payConfirm去支付

```
<div class="item-pay">
                <h3>选择以下支付方式付款</h3>
                <div class="pay-way">
                    <p>支付平台</p>
                    <div class="pay pay-ali" :class="{'checked':payType==1}" @click="payTypeSelect(1)"></div>
                    <div class="pay pay-wechat" :class="{'checked':payType==2}" @click="payTypeSelect(2)"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="pay-confirm fr">
                    <el-button type="danger" class="confirm-button" @click="payConfirm()">确认支付</el-button>
                </div>
            </div>
```

### 16.7 支付宝支付成功后端

https://opendocs.alipay.com/common/02kf5q

修改payment/views.py

添加支付宝支付成功方法

```
class AliPaySuccView(APIView):
    permission_classes = [IsAuthenticated]

    def put(self, request):
        data = request.query_params.dict()  # QueryDict->dict
        signature = data.pop('sign')

        app_private_key_string = open(
            os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "keys/app_private_key.pem")).read()
        alipay_public_key_string = open(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)),
                                                     "keys/alipay_public_key.pem")).read()

        alipay_client = AliPay(
            appid=settings.ALIPAY_APPID,  # 应用APPID
            # appid='2016092500594764', # 应用APPID
            app_notify_url=None,  # 默认回调url
            app_private_key_string=app_private_key_string,
            alipay_public_key_string=alipay_public_key_string,  # 支付宝的公钥，验证支付宝回传消息使用，不是你自己的公钥,
            sign_type="RSA2",  # RSA 或者 RSA2
            debug=settings.ALIPAY_DEBUG  # 默认False
        )


        success = alipay_client.verify(data, signature)

        if not success:
            return Response({'message': '非法参数请求'}, status=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN)


        user = request.user
        order_id = data.get('out_trade_no')
        try:
            order = OrderInfo.objects.get(
                order_id=order_id,
                user=user,
                status=OrderInfo.ORDER_STATUS_ENUM['UNPAID'], # 待支付
            )
        except OrderInfo.DoesNotExist:
            return Response({'message': '无效的订单信息'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        # 保存支付结果
        # 获取支付交易号
        trade_id = data.get('trade_no')
        Payment.objects.create(
            order=order,
            trade_id=trade_id
        )

        # 更改订单的状态
        order.status = OrderInfo.ORDER_STATUS_ENUM['UNSEND'] # 待发货
        order.pay_method = OrderInfo.PAY_METHODS_ENUM['ALIPAY']
        order.save()


        return Response({'trade_id': trade_id})
```



修改payment/urls.py

添加支付成功url

```
urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'^payment/alipay-succ/$', views.AliPaySuccView.as_view()),
]
```

修改api/order.js 

添加aliPaySucc 支付成功的回调页面

```
const aliPaySucc = (params) => {
    return axios.put('/payment/alipay-succ/' + params , '', {
        headers: {
            Authorization: 'JWT ' + getToken()
        }
    })
}
```



修改Order/AliPaySucc.vue

调用后端接口获取trade_id并且显示在页面

```
<template>
    <div class="order-pay">
        <order-header title="支付完成"></order-header>
        <div class="wrapper">
            <div class="order-wrap">
                <div class="item-order">
                    <div class="icon-succ"></div>
                    <div class="order-info">
                        <h2>订单支付成功</h2>
                        <p>订单编号: <span>{{trade_id}}</span></p>
                        <p>点击<span>此处</span>查看订单信息</p>
                    </div>
                </div>

            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</template>
<script>
    import OrderHeader from '@/components/common/OperHeader.vue'
    import { aliPaySucc } from '@/api/Order'


    export default{
        name:'order-pay',
        data(){
            return {
                trade_id: ''
            }
        },
        components:{
            OrderHeader
        },
        methods:{
            _aliPaySucc() {
                let params = document.location.search
                aliPaySucc(params).then(res => {
                    this.trade_id = res.trade_id
                }).catch(function (err) {
                    console.log(err)
                })
            },
        },
        mounted() {
            this._aliPaySucc()
        }
    }
</script>
```

        path: 'alipay-success',
        name: 'alipay-success',
        component: AliPaySucc,
        meta: { requiresAuth: true }
      },
```

修改settings/dev.py

```
# Haystack
HAYSTACK_CONNECTIONS = {
    'default': {
        'ENGINE': 'haystack.backends.elasticsearch7_backend.Elasticsearch7SearchEngine',
        'URL': 'http://192.168.70.101:9200/',  # 此处为elasticsearch运行的服务器ip地址，端口号固定为9200
        'INDEX_NAME': 'xiaofu',  # 指定elasticsearch建立的索引库的名称
    },
}

# 当添加、修改、删除数据时，自动生成索引
HAYSTACK_SIGNAL_PROCESSOR = 'haystack.signals.RealtimeSignalProcessor'
```





### 17.3 搜索后端



```
INSTALLED_APPS = [
	'haystack',
]
```



新建goods/search_indexes.py

```
from haystack import indexes

from goods.models import Sku


class SkuIndex(indexes.SearchIndex, indexes.Indexable):

    # document=True：说明text字段是索引字段
    # use_template=True：说明索引字段中包含哪些内容会在一个文件中进行指定
    text = indexes.CharField(document=True, use_template=True)
    id = indexes.IntegerField(model_attr='id')
    name = indexes.CharField(model_attr='name')
    sub_title = indexes.CharField(model_attr='sub_title')



    def get_model(self):
        return Sku

    def index_queryset(self, using=None):
        return self.get_model().objects.filter(is_online=True)
```

修改goods/serializers.py

```
from .search_indexes import SkuIndex
from drf_haystack.serializers import HaystackSerializer

class SkuIndexSerializer(HaystackSerializer):
    object = SkuSerializer(read_only=True)
    
    class Meta:
        index_classes = [SkuIndex]
        fields = ('text', 'object')
```



修改goods/views.py

```
from drf_haystack.viewsets import HaystackViewSet
from .serializers import SkuSerializer, BannerSerializer, SkuIndexSerializer

class SkuSearchViewSet(HaystackViewSet):
    index_models = [Sku]
    serializer_class = SkuIndexSerializer
    pagination_class = StandardPagination
```



修改goods/urls.py

```
router = routers.DefaultRouter()
router.register('goods/search', views.SkuSearchViewSet, basename='skus_search')



urlpatterns += router.urls
```

修改Search.vue 

使用computed 计算搜索文字，使用watch查看路由和搜索关键字

引入后端getSearchList

```
<template>
    <div>
        <div class="product-box">
            <div class="container">
                <div class="wrapper">
                    <div class="list-box" >
                        <div class="list" v-if="count>0">
                            <div class="item" v-for="good in goods">
                                <div class="item-img"><img :src="good.object.default_image_url" alt=""></div>
                                <div class="item-info">
                                    <p>{{good.object.name}}</p>
                                    <p class="price">¥{{good.object.sale_price}}元</p>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div v-else>
                            未搜索到数据
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    import { getSearchList } from '@/api/Goods'


    export default {
        name: "Search",
        data() {
            return {
                page_size: 4,
                count: 0,
                goods: []
            }
        },
        computed: {
            q: {
                get: function () {
                    return this.$route.query.q
                },
                set: function (newValue) {

                }

            }
        },
        watch: {
            q (newVal,oldVal) {
                this.page = 1
                this._getGoodsList()
            }
    },

        methods: {
            _getGoodsList() {

                let params = {
                    text: this.q,
                    page: this.page,
                    page_size: this.page_size,
                }
                getSearchList(params).then(res => {
                    this.count = res.count;
                    this.goods = res.results
                })

            },
        },
        created() {
            this._getGoodsList()
        }
    }
</script>

                                background-color:#7ECF68;
                            }
                            &.kill-pro{
                                background-color:#E82626;
                            }
                        }
                        .item-img {
                            img {
                                width: 100%;
                                height: 205px;
                            }
                        }
                        .item-info {
                            padding 0 10px;
                            p {
                                color: 26px;

### 17.5 前端无限加载

```
E:\讲课代码\vue\vue2 课程准备\xiaofu>npm i vue-infinite-scroll --save
```



修改goods/Search.vue

引入vue-infinite-scroll

```
<div class="scroll-more"
                     v-infinite-scroll="scrollMore"
                     infinite-scroll-disabled="busy"
                     infinite-scroll-distance="120"
                >
                    <img src="/imgs/loading-svg/loading-spinning-bubbles.svg" alt="" v-show="loading">
                </div>
```



在methods中修改_getGoodsList 下的getSearchList里添加showNextPage, busy等



scrollMore 判断是否还有下一页，如果有则无限加载

watch中添加this.goods = []

```
    import infiniteScroll from 'vue-infinite-scroll'
	data() {
    	return {
            loading:false,
            busy: false,
            showNextPage: true,
            }
        },
        directives: {infiniteScroll},

	watch: {
            q (newVal, oldVal) {
                this.page = 1
                this.goods = []
                this._getGoodsList()
            }
        },


	methods: {
            _getGoodsList() {
                this.loading = true
                let params = {
                    text: this.q,
                    page: this.page,
                    page_size: this.page_size
                }
                getSearchList(params).then(res => {
                    this.count = res.count;
                    // this.goods = res.results
                    this.goods = this.goods.concat(res.results)
                    this.loading = false;
                    this.showNextPage = res.next
                    this.busy = false
                })
            },
            scrollMore() {
                this.busy = true
                if(this.showNextPage){
                    setTimeout(()=> {
                        this.page++
                        // this._getNextPageList()
                        this._getGoodsList()
                    },2000)
                }

            },
    }        
```

<template>
    <div class="reset-form">
        <div class="reset-box">
            <el-form ref="formValidate" label-position="right" :model="formValidate" label-width="100px" :rules="ruleValidate">
                <el-form-item label="用户名" prop="username">
                    <el-input v-model="formValidate.username" clearable size="large"  placeholder="邮箱 / 用户名 / 登陆手机"></el-input>
                </el-form-item>
                <el-form-item label="验证码" prop="captcha" class="img_code">

                            <img :src="image_code_url" @click="get_captcha" alt="图形验证码" class="pic_code">

<script>
    import config from '@/config'

    const baseUrl = process.env.NODE_ENV ==='development' ? config.baseUrl.dev : config.baseUrl.pro
    export default {
        name: "index",
        data() {
            return {
                image_code_url: '',
                formValidate: {
                    username: '',
                    captcha: '',
                },
                ruleValidate: {
                    username: [
                        {required: true, message: '用户名不能为空', trigger: 'blur'},
                        {type: 'string', min: 4, max: 30, message: '用户名长度为4-30字符', trigger: 'blur'},

                    ],
                    captcha: [
                        {required: true, message: '验证码不能为空', trigger: 'blur'},
                        {type: 'string', min: 4, max: 4, message: '验证码为4位', trigger: 'blur'}
                    ],
                }
            }
        },
        methods: {
            get_captcha() {
                let uuid = this.$uuid.v4()
                this.uuid = uuid
                this.image_code_url = baseUrl + '/captcha/' + uuid + '/';
            },
        },
        mounted() {
            this.get_captcha()
        }

    }
</script>

### 18.2  itsdangerous模块使用

我们使用itsdangerous模块做手机号的加解密，

```

```



```
from itsdangerous import TimedJSONWebSignatureSerializer
from django.conf import settings

SECRET_KEY = 'django-insecure-!ze^us7_a26y$8+3_dqi(f)s9bsdlpwrsr=c$x%o_q+z@#gv4&'


serializer = TimedJSONWebSignatureSerializer(SECRET_KEY, 300)
token = serializer.dumps({'mobile': '13888889999'})
token = token.decode()
print("token",token)

try:
    data = serializer.loads(token)
    print(data)
except:
    print("error")

### 18.3 后端实现忘记密码第一步

修改users/models.py

添加方法create_sms_token

```
from itsdangerous import TimedJSONWebSignatureSerializer
from verifications.constants import SMS_CODE_EXPIRE
from django.conf import settings

    def create_sms_token(self):
        serializer = TimedJSONWebSignatureSerializer(settings.SECRET_KEY, SMS_CODE_EXPIRE)
        data = {
            'mobile': self.mobile
        }
        access_token = serializer.dumps(data)
        return access_token.decode()
```



修改users/views.py

添加checkUserExist根据输入的手机或者用户名或者email检查用户是否存在

如果存在则返回access_token以及mobile

```
from .utils import get_user


class UserViewSet(ModelViewSet):
	@action(methods=['post'], detail=False, url_path='check-user-exist', url_name='check-user-exist', name='check-user-exist')
    def checkUserExist(self, request):
        serializer = self.get_serializer(data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)

        username = request.data.get("username")
        user = get_user(username)

        if user is None:
            return Response({"message": "用户不存在"}, status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)
        access_token = user.create_sms_token()
        mobile = user.mobile
        mobile = mobile[0:2] + "*" * 7 + mobile[-2:]
        return Response({'mobile': mobile, 'access_token': access_token})
        
        
    def get_serializer_class(self):
    	elif self.action == 'checkUserExist':
            return CaptchaSerializer
```



![](水印pics\重置密码第一步后端.png)



### 18.4 前端实现忘记密码第一步

修改store/modules/user.js

state下添加passReset

mutations下添加SET_PASS_RESET_STEP，SET_ACCESS_TOKEN，SET_ENCRYPT_MOBILE

```
passReset: {
            access_token: '',
            encrypted_mobile: '',
            passResetStep: 0
        }
        
        
        SET_PASS_RESET_STEP:  (state, step) => {
            state.passReset.passResetStep = step;
        },
        SET_ACCESS_TOKEN: (state, access_token) => {
            state.passReset.access_token = access_token
        },
        SET_ENCRYPT_MOBILE: (state, encrypted_mobile) => {
            state.passReset.encrypted_mobile = encrypted_mobile
        }
```



修改api/Account.js 

添加检查用户是否存在后端

```
// 第一步检查用户是否存在
const checkUserExist = (data) => {
    return axios.post('/users/check-user-exist/', data)
}


export { checkUserExist }
```



修改Resetpass/Index.vue

按钮点击后调用checkUserExist

增加checkUser接口

```
<el-button type="danger" class="confirm_but" size="large" @click="checkUser('formValidate')">确定</el-button>

import { mapMutations } from "vuex";
import { checkUserExist } from '@/api/Account'

		checkUser(name) {
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let post_data = {
                            "username": this.formValidate.username,
                            "captcha": this.formValidate.captcha,
                            "uuid": this.uuid,
                        }
                        checkUserExist(post_data).then(res => {
                            this.SET_PASS_RESET_STEP(1)
                            this.SET_ACCESS_TOKEN(res.access_token)
                            this.SET_ENCRYPT_MOBILE(res.mobile)
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            console.log(err)
                        })
                    }
                })
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_PASS_RESET_STEP','SET_ACCESS_TOKEN','SET_ENCRYPT_MOBILE'])
```





修改views/ResetPass.vue

使用watch和computed来监控passResetStep并且调用对应组件

```
watch: {
            passResetStep (newVal, oldVal ) {
                if (newVal==1) {
                    this.currentComp = 'Process'
                }
            }
        },

        computed: {
            ...mapState({'passResetStep': state=>state.user.passReset.passResetStep})
        },
```

新建Resetpass/Sms.vue

机密的手机号在created中从state获取到，另外手机输入input需要设置为disabled

引入mapstate 里的加密手机号

基础页面

```
<template>
    <div class="info-form">
        <el-form ref="formValidate" label-position="right" :model="formValidate" label-width="80px" :rules="ruleValidate">
            <el-form-item label="手机号" prop="encrypted_mobile">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.encrypted_mobile" clearable size="large" disabled></el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-form-item label="验证码" prop="sms_code">
                <el-input v-model="formValidate.sms_code" size="large"  placeholder="请输入验证码">
                    <el-button style="width:150px" :disabled="sms_disable" ref="sms_button" slot="append" @click="getSmsCode">{{sms_code_tip}}</el-button>
                </el-input>
            </el-form-item>
            <el-button type="danger"  style="width: 100%"  @click="handleSubmit('formValidate')">下一步</el-button>
        </el-form>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    import { mapState } from 'vuex';
    export default {
        name: "CheckPhone",
        data () {
            return {
                formValidate: {
                    encrypted_mobile: '',
                    sms_code: ''
                },
                ruleValidate: {
                    sms_code: [
                        { required: true, message: '请填写验证码', trigger: 'blur' },
                        { type: 'string', min: 6, max: 6, message: '验证码长度错误', trigger: 'blur' }
                    ]
                },
                sms_code_tip: "获取短信验证码",
                send_sms_flag: true,
                sms_disable: false

            };
        },
        
        methods: {
            getSmsCode () {
                if (this.send_sms_flag) {
                    let second = 10;
                    this.sms_code_tip = second + '秒后重新获取';
                    let t = setInterval(() => {
                        if (second === 1) { // 倒计时即将结束
                            clearInterval(t); // 停止回调函数的执行
                            this.sms_disable = false
                            this.sms_code_tip = '获取短信验证码'; // 还原sms_code_tip的提示文字
                        } else { // 正在倒计时
                            second -= 1; // num = num - 1;
                            this.sms_code_tip = second + '秒后重新获取';
                            this.sms_disable = true
                        }
                    }, 1000)
                }
            },
        },
        
    }
</script>

<style lang="stylus" scoped>
    .info-form
        width 80%

</style>
```

<template>
    <div>
        <!--  使用element ui步骤条      -->
        <div class="progress">
            <el-steps  :active="forgetPassStep" finish-status="success" align-center>
                <el-step title="验证手机号"></el-step>
                <el-step title="重置密码"></el-step>
                <el-step title="完成"></el-step>
            </el-steps>
        </div>

        <!--  动态显示组件      -->
        <div class="forget-pass-box">
            <transition mode="out-in">
                <component :is="currentProcessCom"></component>
            </transition>
        </div>
    </div>

</template>

<script>
    import { mapState } from "vuex";
    import Sms from '@/components/Account/ResetPass/Sms'

    export default {
        name: "process",
        components: {
            Sms
        },
        data() {
            return {
                active: 0,          // 当前的步骤
                currentProcessCom: 'Sms'   // 当前显示的组件
            };
        },
        updated() {
            if (this.forgetPassStep==1){
                this.currentProcessCom = 'ChangePass'
            }
            if (this.forgetPassStep==3){
                this.currentProcessCom = 'Done'
            }
        },
        computed: {
            ...mapState({'forgetPassStep': state=>state.user.passReset.forgetPassStep})
        },
    }
</script>

### 18.6 后端借助access_token发送短信验证码

修改users/models.py

在class User(AbstractUser)下新增静态方法check_access_token

```
from itsdangerous import BadData

@staticmethod
    def check_access_token(access_token):
        serializer = TimedJSONWebSignatureSerializer(settings.SECRET_KEY, SMS_CODE_EXPIRE)
        try:
            data = serializer.loads(access_token)
        except BadData:
            return None
        else:
            mobile = data.get('mobile')
            return mobile
```

修改verifications/views.py 添加SMSCodeByAccessTokenView

```
# 通过access_token 解密出手机号随后发送短信
class SMSCodeByAccessTokenView(GenericAPIView):
    def get(self, request):
        # 获取access_token
        access_token = request.query_params.get('access_token')
        if not access_token:
            return Response({'message':'没有access token 请检查'},status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        # 获取手机号
        mobile = User.check_access_token(access_token)
        if mobile is None:
            return Response({'message':'非法access token 请检查'},status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        sms_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes',mobile)
        sms_code = sms_obj.generate_code()
        # sms_obj.send_sms_code(sms_code)
        return Response({'message': "发送短信验证码成功"}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
        # return Response({ 'mobile': mobile },status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
```



修改verifications/urls.py

添加路由

```
re_path(r'sms/$', views.SMSCodeByAccessTokenView.as_view()),
```

```
import { tokenSms } from '@/api/Account'

getSmsCode () {
	let params = {"access_token": this.access_token}
                    tokenSms(params).then(res => {
                        this.$message.success(res.message)
                    }).catch(function(err){
                        this.sms_disable = false
                    })
}

computed: {
            ...mapState({'access_token': state=>state.user.passReset.access_token})
        },
```

### 18.8 后端进行短信验证码验证

修改verifications/views.py

```
class CheckSmsCodeByTokenView(APIView):
    def post(self,request):
        access_token = request.data.get('access_token');
        sms_code = request.data.get('sms_code');

        if not access_token:
            return Response({'message': '没有access token 请检查'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        mobile = User.check_access_token(access_token)
        if mobile is None:
            return Response({'message': '非法access token 请检查'}, status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)

        sms_obj = CodeDeal('verify_codes', mobile)
        sms_obj.verify_code(sms_code)
        return Response({'detail': '短信验证成功'}, status=status.HTTP_200_OK)
```



修改verifications/urls.py

添加sms-check-bytoken

```
   re_path(r'sms-check-bytoken/$', views.CheckSmsCodeByTokenView.as_view()),

```



![](水印pics\通过token验证短信验证码.png)

    import {  smsCheckByToken } from "@/api/Account";


handleSubmit (name) { // 提交验证
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let data = {"access_token":this.access_token, "sms_code": this.formValidate.sms_code}
                        smsCheckByToken(data).then(res => {
                            this.SET_FORGET_PASS_STEP(1);
                        }).catch(function(err){
                            that.sms_disable = false
                        })
                    } else {
                        this.$message.error({
                            message: '请填写正确的验证码',
                            closable: true
                        });
                    }
                });
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_FORGET_PASS_STEP']),
```

### 18.10 后端实现重置密码

修改users/serializers.py

添加PassUpdateSerializer

```
class PassUpdateSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    """
    更新密码
    """
    password_confirm = serializers.CharField(label='确认密码', write_only=True)

    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ('id', 'password', 'password_confirm' )



    def validate(self, data):
        # 判断两次密码
        if data['password'] != data['password_confirm']:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('两次输入的密码不一致')

        access_token = self.context['view'].kwargs['access_token']
        mobile = User.check_access_token(access_token)

        if mobile is None:
            raise serializers.ValidationError('非法的access_token')

        return data
```



修改users/views.py

添加 PassUpdateView

```
from rest_framework.generics import UpdateAPIView
from .serializers import PassUpdateSerializer

class PassUpdateView(UpdateAPIView):
    serializer_class = PassUpdateSerializer

    def get_object(self):
        access_token = self.request.parser_context.get('kwargs').get('access_token')
        mobile = User.check_access_token(access_token)
        user = get_user(mobile)
        return user
    #
    def update(self, request, *args, **kwargs):
        try:
            instance = self.get_object()
        except:
            return Response({"detail": "非法的access_token"})
        serializer = self.get_serializer(instance, data=request.data)
        serializer.is_valid(raise_exception=True)
        self.perform_update(serializer)
        instance.set_password(request.data.get("password"))
        instance.save()
        return Response({"detail": "更新成功"})
```



修改users/urls.py

添加修改密码路由

```
   re_path(r'^update-pass/(?P<access_token>\S*)$', views.PassUpdateView.as_view()),
```

import { updatePass } from '@/api/Account'
    import {mapMutations, mapState} from "vuex";

resetPass(name) {
                var that = this
                this.$refs[name].validate((valid) => {
                    if (valid) {
                        let access_token = this.access_token
                        let data = {"password": this.formValidate.password,  "password_confirm": this.formValidate.password_confirm}

                        updatePass(access_token,data).then(res => {
                            this.SET_FORGET_PASS_STEP(3);
                        }).catch(function(err){

                        })
                    } else {
                        this.$message.error({
                            message: '请填写正确的信息',
                            closable: true
                        });
                    }
                })
            },
            ...mapMutations(['SET_FORGET_PASS_STEP']),
            
            computed: {
            ...mapState({'access_token': state=>state.user.passReset.access_token})
        },

新建ResetPass/Done.vue

```
<template>
    <div class="done">
        <div class="info">
            <span>修改密码成功</span>
            <span class="sec">{{count}}</span>
            <span>秒后跳转</span>
            <router-link to="/" class="home">首页</router-link>
        </div>
    </div>
</template>

<script>
    export default {
        name: "Done",
        data() {
            return {
                count: 0
            }
        },
        methods: {
            goHome() {
                let second = 10
                this.count = second
                let t = setInterval(() => {
                    if (second === 1) {
                        clearInterval(t)
                        this.$router.push('/')
                    } else {
                        second -= 1
                        this.count = second
                    }
                },1000)
            }
        },
        mounted() {
            this.goHome()
        }

    }
</script>

<style lang="stylus" scoped>
    .done
        display flex
        justify-content center
        align-items center
        width 90%
        height 150%
        background-color: #fff
        .sec
            color red
        .info
            font-size 24px
        .home
            color red
</style>
```









# 19 第三方登录

### 19.1 后端获取Authorization Code

新建app  oauth

```
(xiaofu) [apps@centos1 apps]$ python ../../manage.py startapp oauth
```



新建模型类oauth/model.py

```
from django.db import models
from xiaofu.utils.models import BaseModel

class OAuthQQUser(BaseModel):
    user = models.ForeignKey('users.User', on_delete=models.CASCADE, verbose_name='对应用户')
    openid = models.CharField(max_length=64, verbose_name='openid', db_index=True)

    class Meta:
        db_table = 'tb_oauth'
        verbose_name = 'QQ登录'
        verbose_name_plural = verbose_name
```





新建oauth/utils.py

```
from django.conf import settings
from urllib.parse import urlencode


class OAuthQQ():
    # 对openid进行加解密的安全密钥
    SECRET_KEY = settings.SECRET_KEY
    # 对openid加密之后生成的access_token的有效时间
    EXPIRES_IN = 10 * 60

    def __init__(self, client_id=None, app_key=None, redirect_uri=None, state='/'):
        # 申请QQ登录成功后，分配给应用的appid。
        self.client_id = client_id or settings.QQ_APP_ID
        # APP Key
        self.app_key = app_key or settings.QQ_APP_KEY
        # 回调url
        self.redirect_uri = redirect_uri or settings.QQ_REDIRECT_URI

        self.state = state

    def get_login_url(self):
        # qq登录所需参数
        url = 'https://graph.qq.com/oauth2.0/authorize?'
        params = {
            'response_type': 'code',
            'client_id': self.client_id,
            'redirect_uri': self.redirect_uri,
            'state': self.state,
        }

        url += urlencode(params)

        return url
```





新建oauth/views.py

```
from django.shortcuts import render
from rest_framework.views import APIView
from rest_framework.response import Response
# Create your views here.

from .utils import OAuthQQ

class OAuthQQView(APIView):
    def get(self, request):
        # 获取网页下一跳参数next
        next = request.query_params.get('next', '/')

        oauth_qq = OAuthQQ(state=next)
        qq_login_url = oauth_qq.get_login_url()


        return Response({'qq_login_url': qq_login_url})
```



修改最外层urls.py

添加oauth路由

```
    path('oauth/', include('oauth.urls')),
```



新建oauth/urls.py

```
from django.urls import path,include,re_path
from rest_framework_jwt.views import obtain_jwt_token, refresh_jwt_token
from rest_framework import routers
from . import views


urlpatterns = [
   re_path(r'^qq/auth/$', views.OAuthQQView.as_view()),

]
```
